It combines order flow microstructure, cross-market lead-lag, regime-adaptive modeling, and confidence gating to achieve a tradeable edge.\n     6→\n     7→**Realistic expectations** (from 500K+ words of research):\n     8→- Directional accuracy: 52-56% at 5-min horizon\n     9→- Backtest-to-live Sharpe degradation: 50-70% (need Sharpe >2.0 in backtest to survive)\n    10→- Round-trip costs: 8-12 bps minimum\n    11→- Alpha half-life: 1-6 months for ML patterns\n    12→- Optimal feature count: 18-25 (not 200+)\n    13→\n    14→## Tech Stack\n    15→\n    16→| Component | Choice | Why |\n    17→|-----------|--------|-----|\n    18→| Language | Python 3.12+ | ML ecosystem, async support |\n    19→| Package manager | uv | Fast, deterministic (never pip/poetry) |\n    20→| Primary model | LightGBM | Outperforms XGBoost by 0.5-1.5% on 5-min crypto |\n    21→| Secondary model | CatBoost | Ordered boosting prevents leakage, adds diversity |\n    22→| Sequence model | GRU (PyTorch) | Hidden state extracted as features for LightGBM |\n    23→| Ensemble | Stacking (logistic regression meta-learner) | 2-5% over best single model |\n    24→| Regime detection | Hierarchical (HMM + BOCPD + GARCH + Efficiency Ratio) | Faster detection than HMM alone |\n    25→| Exchange data | ccxt (WebSocket + REST) | Binance WS for klines/depth/trades, Bybit for derivatives |\n    26→| Cross-market | yfinance, Twelve Data | NQ, Gold, DXY (15-min delayed, acceptable) |\n    27→| On-chain | mempool.space WS | Whale detection only (on-chain operates at 4h+, not 5-min) |\n    28→| Logging | structlog | Structured JSON logs, never print() |\n    29→| API | FastAPI + uvicorn | Prediction endpoints, health, metrics |\n    30→| Database | SQLite (dev) -> TimescaleDB (prod) | Zero setup for dev |\n    31→| Inference | ONNX Runtime | 2-5x speedup over native |\n    32→| Tuning | Optuna | MedianPruner, Sharpe objective |\n    33→| Testing | pytest + pytest-cov | Required for every feature computation |\n    34→| Linting | ruff + mypy (strict) | Type safety, code quality |\n    35→\n    36→## Key Architecture Decisions\n    37→\n    38→These decisions are the result of extensive research (49 files in `research/`). Do NOT change them without reviewing the corresponding ADR in `DECISIONS.md`.\n    39→\n    40→### Model Architecture\n    41→- **LightGBM over XGBoost** (ADR-001): Faster training, better accuracy on crypto tick data\n    42→- **Stacking ensemble over per-regime models** (ADR-006): Per-regime models fragment scarce data. Single ensemble with regime as input feature is more robust\n    43→- **Ternary target (up/flat/down) with adaptive threshold** (ADR-002): Acknowledges untradeable low-volatility periods. Threshold adapts per regime\n    44→- **Triple barrier labeling over fixed threshold** (ADR-008): Accounts for time decay and stop-loss, produces more realistic labels\n    45→\n    46→### Data & Features\n    47→- **Dual normalization pipeline** (ADR in RESEARCH_SYNTHESIS.md): Raw features for tree models (normalization harms trees), robust scaling + rank-to-gaussian for neural models\n    48→- **On-chain as regime context only, not primary signal** (ADR-004): On-chain signals operate at 4h-24h, not 5-min\n    49→- **Skip real-time sentiment, use funding rate** (ADR-005): NLP sentiment too slow for 5-min. Funding rate is the only useful \"sentiment\" at this timeframe\n    50→- **Feature priority**: Microstructure (OBI, OFI, microprice) captures 60-80% of achievable 5-min signal\n    51→\n    52→### Validation & Risk\n    53→- **Purged walk-forward validation**: 14-day sliding window, 18-bar purge (90 min), 12-bar embargo (60 min). Sliding, NOT expanding (crypto non-stationarity)\n    54→- **Confidence gating pipeline**: isotonic calibration -> meta-labeling -> conformal prediction -> adaptive threshold -> drawdown gate. This is the single biggest Sharpe multiplier (2-4x)\n    55→- **Quarter-Kelly position sizing**: Position size = 0.25 * Kelly fraction * confidence score\n    56→- **Annualization**: sqrt(105,120) for 24/7 crypto. 288 bars/day * 365 days = 105,120 bars/year. NEVER use sqrt(252)\n    57→\n    58→### Infrastructure\n    59→- **asyncio single-process architecture** (ADR-010): All collectors and processing in one event loop\n    60→- **Event-driven backtest engine with Numba** (ADR-009): 100x faster than pure Python, realistic fills\n    61→- **Numpy ring buffers** for data structures: 10-20x less memory than pandas DataFrames on hot path\n    62→\n    63→## Code Conventions\n    64→\n    65→### Mandatory Rules\n    66→1. **Named exports only** - never use `export default` or bare module-level assignments\n    67→2. **structlog for all logging** - never use `print()` for any output\n    68→3. **Parameterized SQL queries only** - never use f-strings or string interpolation for SQL\n    69→4. **All features must use only past data** - no look-ahead bias. Every feature computation at time t may only use data from times <= t\n    70→5. **Type hints on all functions** - mypy strict mode is enforced\n    71→6. **Tests required for every feature computation** - including golden dataset tests against hand-verified values\n    72→7. **No `any` types** - be explicit with all type annotations\n    73→8. **No TODO/FIXME/HACK without linked issue** - if you must leave one, create a GitHub issue first\n    74→9. **Secrets via environment variables** - never commit API keys, never use .env files in repo\n    75→\n    76→### Error Handling\n    77→- Always use try/catch with meaningful error messages at system boundaries\n    78→- Never swallow errors silently - log with context via structlog\n    79→- Never fire-and-forget async operations - track completion\n    80→- Health endpoints must check actual dependencies, not just return \"ok\"\n    81→\n    82→### Feature Engineering Rules\n    83→- Every feature must be tested for look-ahead bias (shuffle test + truncation test)\n    84→- Rolling calculations use only past data (no centered windows)\n    85→- NaN handling: forward-fill for price data, zero for counts, drop for model input\n    86→- All normalization fitted on training data only, per fold\n    87→\n    88→### Commit Hygiene\n    89→- Meaningful commit messages explaining WHY, not just WHAT\n    90→- Pass lint + typecheck + test before committing\n    91→- One logical change per commit, max 5 commits per feature\n    92→- Build one feature, verify, commit - never batch 5 features\n    93→\n    94→## Project Structure\n    95→\n    96→```\n    97→ep2-crypto/\n    98→├── CLAUDE.md                    # THIS FILE - project context for AI sessions\n    99→├── PLAN.md                      # Original development plan (Phase 0-11)\n   100→├── RESEARCH_SYNTHESIS.md        # Distilled findings from 49 research files\n   101→├── BACKTESTING_PLAN.md          # Comprehensive backtesting methodology\n   102→├── SPRINTS.md                   # Sprint planning with acceptance criteria\n   103→├── REQUIREMENTS.md              # Functional and non-functional requirements\n   104→├── DECISIONS.md                 # Architecture Decision Records (ADR-001 to ADR-010)\n   105→├── pyproject.toml               # Dependencies and tool configuration\n   106→├── uv.lock                      # Locked dependencies\n   107→├── research/                    # 49 research files (read-only reference)\n   108→│   ├── meta_labeling_deep_research.md\n   109→│   ├── microstructure_ofi_microprice.md\n   110→│   ├── monte_carlo_validation.md\n   111→│   ├── retraining_strategies.md\n   112→│   ├── statistical_validation_tests.py\n   113→│   ├── STRESS_TESTING.md\n   114→│   ├── transaction_cost_modeling.md\n   115→│   └── ... (42 more research files)\n   116→├── src/\n   117→│   └── ep2_crypto/\n   118→│       ├── __init__.py\n   119→│       ├── config.py                  # Pydantic Settings, env-var based\n   120→│       ├── db/\n   121→│       │   ├── schema.py              # SQLite/TimescaleDB schema\n   122→│       │   └── repository.py          # Parameterized query layer\n   123→│       ├── ingest/\n   124→│       │   ├── base.py                # Base collector interface\n   125→│       │   ├── exchange.py            # Binance WS: klines, depth@100ms, aggTrades\n   126→│       │   ├── derivatives.py         # Bybit: OI, funding, liquidations\n   127→│       │   ├── onchain.py             # mempool.space: whale detection\n   128→│       │   ├── cross_market.py        # NQ, Gold, DXY, ETH\n   129→│       │ ├── base.py                # Feature pipeline interface\n   133→│       │   ├── microstructure.py      # OBI, OFI, microprice, spread, TFI\n   134→│       │   ├── volume.py              # Volume delta, VWAP deviation, rate-of-change\n   135→│       │   ├── volatility.py          # Realized, Parkinson, EWMA, vol-of-vol\n   136→│       │   ├── momentum.py            # ROC, RSI, linreg slope, quantile rank\n   137→│       │   ├── cross_market.py        # Lead-lag, correlation, divergence\n   138→│       │   ├── temporal.py            # Cyclical encoding, session, time-to-funding\n   139→│       │   ├── regime_features.py     # ER, GARCH vol, HMM probs as features\n   140→│       │   ├── normalization.py       # Dual pipeline (raw for trees, robust for neural)\n   141→│       │   └── pipeline.py            # Combines all feature sets\n   142→│       ├── regime/\n   143→│       │   ├── detector.py            # Hierarchical regime detection\n   144→│       │   ├── hmm.py                 # 2-state GaussianHMM\n   145→│       │   ├── bocpd.py               # Bayesian Online Change Point Detection\n   146→│       │   ├── garch.py               # GJR-GARCH(1,1)-t conditional volatility\n   147→│       │   └── efficiency_ratio.py    # Kaufman Efficiency Ratio\n   148→│       ├── models/\n   149→│       │   ├── lgbm_direction.py      # LightGBM ternary classifier\n   150→│       │   ├── catboost_direction.py  # CatBoost ternary classifier\n   151→│       │   ├── gru_features.py        # GRU hidden state extractor\n   152→│       │   ├── quantile.py            # LightGBM quantile regression (5 quantiles)\n   153→│       │   ├── stacking.py            # Logistic regression meta-learner\n   154→│       │   ├── calibration.py         # Isotonic regression calibration\n   155→│       │   └── tuning.py              # Optuna hyperparameter optimization\n   156→│       ├── confidence/\n   157→│       │   ├── meta_labeling.py       # Meta-labeling gate\n   158→│       │   ├── conformal.py           # Conformal prediction gate\n   159→│       │   ├── gating.py              # Full confidence gating pipeline\n   160→│       │   └── position_sizing.py     # Quarter-Kelly sizing\n   161→│       ├── backtest/\n   162→│       │   ├── walk_forward.py        # Purged walk-forward with embargo\n   163→│       │   ├── engine.py              # Event-driven backtest engine (Numba)\n   164→│       │   ├── cost_engine.py         # Transaction cost modeling (EXISTS)\n   165→│       │   ├── metrics.py             # Sharpe, drawdown, profit factor, etc.\n   166→│       │ data.py\n   170→│       │   ├── engine.py\n   171→│       │   ├── metrics.py\n   172→│       │   ├── statistics.py\n   173→│       │   └── strategies.py\n   174→│       ├── risk/                      # SPRINT 9 — Capital preservation (before backtesting!)\n   175→│       │   ├── position_tracker.py    # Position state, mark-to-market, margin\n   176→│       │   ├── kill_switches.py       # Daily/weekly/drawdown/consecutive loss halts\n   177→│       │   ├── drawdown_gate.py       # Progressive position reduction (3%→15%)\n   178→│       │   ├── volatility_guard.py    # Min/max vol filters, trading hours\n   179→│       │   ├── position_sizer.py      # Quarter-Kelly, ATR stop, max hold period\n   180→│       │   └── risk_manager.py        # Orchestrates all risk components\n   181→│       ├── events/\n   182→│       │   ├── macro.py               # Event-driven macro module (CPI/FOMC)\n   183→│       │   └── cascade.py             # Liquidation cascade detector (Hawkes)\n   184→│       ├── monitoring/\n   185→│       │   ├── alpha_decay.py         # CUSUM, rolling Sharpe, ADWIN\n   186→│       │   └── drift.py               # Feature drift detection (PSI)\n   187→│       └── api/\n   188→│           └── server.py              # FastAPI endpoints\n   189→├── scripts/\n   190→│   ├── collect_history.py             # Backfill historical data\n   191→│   ├── train.py                       # Full training pipeline\n   192→│   ├── backtest.py                    # Run backtests\n   193→│   └── live.py                        # Live prediction loop\n   194→├── tests/\n   195→│   ├── test_features/                 # Feature computation tests\n   196→│   ├── test_models/                   # Model training/inference tests\n   197→│   ├── test_ingest/                   # Data collection tests\n   198→│   ├── test_backtest/                 # Backtesting validation tests\n   199→│   └── test_confidence/               # Gating pipeline tests\n   200→└── docker/\n   201→    ├── Dockerfile\n   202→    └── docker-compose.yml\n   203→```\n   204→\n   205→## How to Run\n   206→\n   207→### Setup\n   208→```bash\n   209→# Install dependencies\n   210→uv sync --all-extras\n   211→\n   212→# Verify installation\n   213→uv run python -c \"import ep2_crypto\"\n   214→```\n   215→\n   216→### Tests\n   217→```bash\n   218→# Run all tests\n   219→uv run pytest\n   220→\n   221→# Run with coverage\n   222→uv run pytest --cov=ep2_crypto --cov-report=term-missing\n   223→\n   224→# Run specific test module\n   225→uv run pytest tests/test_features/\n   226→```\n   227→\n   228→### Linting and Type Checking\n   229→```bash\n   230→# Lint\n   231→uv run ruff check src/ tests/\n   232→\n   233→# Format\n   234→uv run ruff format src/ tests/\n   235→\n   236→# Type check\n   237→uv run mypy src/ep2_crypto/\n   238→```\n   239→\n   240→### Data Collection\n   241→```bash\n   242→# Backfill historical data (60 days OHLCV, OI, funding)\n   243→uv run python scripts/collect_history.py\n   244→\n   245→# Start live data collection\n   246→uv run python scripts/live.py --collect-only\n   247→```\n   248→\n   249→### Training\n   250→```bash\n   251→# Full training pipeline (walk-forward)\n   252→uv run python scripts/train.py\n   253→\n   254→# Hyperparameter tuning\n   255→uv run python scripts/train.py --tune --trials 100\n   256→```\n   257→\n   258→### Backtesting\n   259→```bash\n   260→# Run full backtest with statistical validation\n   261→uv run python scripts/backtest.py\n   262→\n   263→# Run with specific date range\n   264→uv run python scripts/backtest.py --start 2025-01-01 --end 2025-03-01\n   265→```\n   266→\n   267→### API Server\n   268→```bash\n   269→# Start prediction API\n   270→uv run uvicorn ep2_crypto.api.server:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000\n   271→```\n   272→\n   273→## Sprint Process\n   274→\n   275→Development follows 14 sprints defined in `SPRINTS.md`. Each sprint has:\n   276→- Clear objectives and deliverables\n   277→- Acceptance criteria that must pass before moving on\n   278→- Key files to create/modify\n   279→- Dependencies on previous sprints\n   280→\n   281→**Current sprint progress**: See `SPRINTS.md` for status.\n   282→\n   283→## Key Research References\n   284→\n   285→When implementing a module, consult the relevant research files in `research/`:\n   286→\n   287→| Module | Key Research Files |\n   288→|--------|-------------------|\n   289→| Microstructure features | `microstructure_ofi_microprice.md` |\n   290→| Meta-labeling | `meta_labeling_deep_research.md` |\n   291→| Monte Carlo validation | `monte_carlo_validation.md` |\n   292→| Stress testing | `STRESS_TESTING.md` |\n   293→| Transaction costs | `transaction_cost_modeling.md` |\n   294→| Model retraining | `retraining_strategies.md` |\n   295→| Statistical validation | `statistical_validation_tests.py` (executable code) |\n   296→| Full synthesis | `RESEARCH_SYNTHESIS.md` (root) |\n   297→| Backtesting methodology | `BACKTESTING_PLAN.md` (root) |\n   298→| Architecture decisions | `DECISIONS.md` (root) |\n   299→\n   300→## Risk Parameters (Starting Configuration)\n   301→\n   302→| Parameter | Value |\n   303→|-----------|-------|\n   304→| Position size per trade | 4-5% of capital (quarter-Kelly capped) |\n   305→| Daily loss limit | 2-3% of capital |\n   306→| Weekly loss limit | 5% of capital |\n   307→| Max drawdown halt | 15% of capital |\n   308→| Catastrophic stop per trade | 3 ATR |\n   309→| Max open positions | 1 |\n   310→| Max trades per day | 30 |\n   311→| Trading hours | 08:00-21:00 UTC (Europe + US sessions) |\n   312→| Weekend position sizing | -30% reduction |\n   313→| Confidence threshold | 0.60 (starting, adaptive) |\n   314→| Min bar volatility | 15% annualized |\n   315→| Max bar volatility | 150% annualized |\n   316→\n   317→## Critical Numbers\n   318→\n   319→| Parameter | Value |\n   320→|-----------|-------|\n   321→| Annualization factor | sqrt(105,120) = 324.22 (NOT sqrt(252)) |\n   322→| Bars per year | 288/day * 365 = 105,120 |\n   323→| Training window | 14 days (4,032 bars) sliding |\n   324→| Test window | 1 day (288 bars) |\n   325→| Purge size | 18 bars (90 min) |\n   326→| Embargo size | 12 bars (60 min) |\n   327→| Target backtest Sharpe | > 2.0 (to survive 50-70% degradation) |\n   328→| Break-even cost target | Strategy must survive > 15 bps round-trip |\n   329→| Expected live Sharpe | 0.6-1.0 (after degradation) |\n   330→| Round-trip cost assumption | 8-12 bps (conservative) |\n   331→\n   332→## Anti-Patterns to Avoid\n   333→\n   334→1. Never random-split time series data\n   335→2. Never use `bidirectional=True` on GRU (uses future data)\n   336→3. Never use centered rolling windows for features (look-ahead bias)\n   337→4. Never trust >70% directional accuracy without checking for look-ahead bias\n   338→5. Never use SMOTE or other oversampling on time series\n   339→6. Never interpolate missing data (forward-fill or drop only)\n   340→7. Never use global normalization (fit on all data) - always per-fold on training data\n   341→8. Never use expanding window for training - crypto non-stationarity makes old data harmful\n   342→9. Never skip transaction costs in backtest evaluation\n   343→10. Never commit without lint + typecheck + test passing\n   344→\n   345→## Research Reference\n   346→\n   347→All research is in `research/` with `research/INDEX.md` as the master lookup.\n   348→Files follow `RR-{category}-{topic}.md` naming. Key files per area:\n   349→\n   350→| Need to implement... | Read this first |\n   351→|---------------------|-----------------|\n   352→| WebSocket data ingestion | `RR-api-ccxt-exchange-integration.md` |\n   353→| Order book features (OBI, OFI) | `RR-ofi-microprice-implementation.md` |\n   354→| Liquidation cascade detection | `RR-cascade-liquidation-detection-system.md` |\n   355→| Cross-market NQ lead-lag | `RR-crossmarket-lead-lag-correlations.md` |\n   356→| Regime detection (HMM etc) | `RR-regime-detection-methods.md` |\n   357→| LightGBM training | `RR-lightgbm-crypto-tuning.md` |\n   358→| GRU/TCN architecture | `RR-gru-tcn-training-architecture.md` |\n   359→| Meta-labeling | `RR-metalabeling-implementation-guide.md` |\n   360→| Walk-forward validation | `RR-walkforward-validation-methods.md` |\n   361→| Backtesting framework | `RR-backtest-framework-design.md` |\n   362→| Statistical validation | `RR-stats-edge-vs-luck-tests.md` |\n   363→| Transaction costs | `RR-costs-transaction-cost-modeling.md` |\n   364→| Paper trading | `RR-papertrade-system-architecture.md` |\n   365→| Alpha decay monitoring | `RR-decay-edge-disappearance-detection.md` |\n   366→\n   367→## Pre-Code Checklists\n   368→\n   369→### Before writing ANY feature computation:\n   370→- [ ] Does it use ONLY data at times <= t? (no look-ahead)\n   371→- [ ] Is it tested with a truncation test? (compute on data[:150] matches data[:200] at index 150)\n   372→- [ ] Does it have a unit test with known input/output?\n   373→- [ ] Is it added to the golden dataset for regression testing?\n   374→- [ ] Is normalization rolling (not global)?\n   375→- [ ] For tree model path: raw value (no normalization)\n   376→- [ ] For neural model path: robust scaling or rank-to-gaussian\n   377→\n   378→### Before writing ANY model training code:\n   379→- [ ] Is the train/val/test split temporal (never random)?\n   380→- [ ] Is early stopping validation carved from training set (not test set)?\n   381→- [ ] Is there a purge gap (18 bars) between train and test?\n   382→- [ ] Is there an embargo (12 bars) after test?\n   383→- [ ] Are sample weights applied (time decay + regime balance)?\n   384→- [ ] Is the target ternary with adaptive threshold?\n   385→\n   386→### Before any backtest evaluation:\n   387→- [ ] Are transaction costs included (8-12 bps round-trip)?\n   388→- [ ] Is execution at next-bar-open (never current-bar-close)?\n   389→- [ ] Is latency simulated (200ms minimum)?\n   390→- [ ] Are funding rate costs modeled for positions held across settlement?\n   391→- [ ] Does the backtest period include at least one bull AND one bear market?\n   392→\n   393→## Session Management\n   394→\n   395→**CRITICAL: Read `PROGRESS.md` at the start of EVERY session.** It has:\n   396→- Current sprint and ticket\n   397→- What was done in previous sessions\n   398→- The EXACT next step to take\n   399→- Any handoff notes from the previous session\n   400→\n   401→Full protocol is in `SESSION_PROTOCOL.md`. Key rules:\n   402→1. One ticket per session is fine — quality over speed\n   403→2. Never read research files unless actively implementing from them (they're 10-50KB)\n   404→3. Update PROGRESS.md at end of session with what was done + exact next step\n   405→4. If context is getting large, wrap up — don't push through\n   406→\n   407→### End-of-Session Handover\n   408→\n   409→At the END of every session, you MUST:\n   410→1. Update PROGRESS.md (what was done, what wasn't, exact next step)\n   411→2. Commit code if any was written\n   412→3. **Generate a handover prompt** for the user to paste in the next session:\n   413→\n   414→```\n   415→Handover prompt for next session:\n   416→---\n   417→Read PROGRESS.md and continue from ticket S{X}-T{Y}. [1-sentence description of what's next].\n   418→Run verification after each ticket. Update PROGRESS.md before ending.\n   419→---\n   420→```\n   421→\n   422→### Sprint Completion Handover\n   423→\n   424→When a sprint is FULLY complete (all tickets `[x]`, acceptance criteria pass):\n   425→1. Commit with message `\"Sprint N complete: <summary>\"`\n   426→2. Decompose the next sprint into tickets in PROGRESS.md\n   427→3. **Generate the sprint handover prompt**:\n   428→\n   429→```\n   430→Sprint N COMPLETE. Start next session with:\n   431→---\n   432→Read PROGRESS.md and start Sprint {N+1}. The tickets are decomposed and ready.\n   433→Current ticket: S{N+1}-T1.   )\n   227→\n   228→    # -- Main entry points ----------------------------------------------------\n   229→\n   230→    def approve_trade(\n   231→        self,\n   232→        signal: TradeDecision:\n   238→        \"\"\"Evaluate whether a trade signal should be executed.\n   239→\n   240→        Runs all risk checks in order:\n   241→            1. Position check (already have one open?)\n   242→            2. Kill switches (any triggered?)\n   243→            3. Max trades per day\n   244→            4. Volatility guard (vol in range? hours ok?)\n   245→            5. Drawdown gate (get multiplier)\n   246→            6. Position sizing (Kelly * confidence * dd_mult * caps)\n   247→            7. Exposure check (within limits?)\n   248→\n   249→        Args:\n   250→            signal: Direction, confidence, and optional Kelly inputs.\n   251→            closes: Full close price array.\n   252→            highs: Full high price array.\n   253→            lows: Full low price array.\n   254→            current_idx: Current bar index.\n   255→\n   256→        Returns:\n   257→            TradeDecision with approval status, size, and stop price.\n   258→        \"\"\"\n   259→        # Step 0: Check if position already open\n   260→        pos = self._position.get_state()\n   261→        if pos.is_open:\n   262→            return self._reject_trade(signal, \"Position already open\")\n   263→\n   264→        # Step 1: Kill switches\n   265→        if self._kill_switches.any_triggered():\n   266→            triggered = self._kill_switches.get_triggered_names()\n   267→            return self._reject_trade(\n   268→                signal,\n   269→                f\"Kill switch(es) triggered: {', '.join(triggered)}\"\n   270→            )\n   271→\n   272→        # Step 2: Max trades per day\n   273→        if self._trades_today >= self._config.max_trades_per_day:\n   274→            return self._reject_trade(\n   275→                signal,\n   276→                f\"Max trades per day reached ({self._trades_today}/\"\n   277→                f\"{self._config.max_trades_per_day})\"\n   278→            )\n   279→\n   280→        # Step 3: Volatility guard\n   281→        vol_state = self._vol_guard.check(\n   282→            closes, current_idx, signal.timestamp_ms\n   283→        )\n   284→        if not vol_state.can_trade:\n   285→            decision = self._reject_trade(\n   286→                signal,\n   287→                vol_state.rejection_reason or \"Volatility guard rejected\",\n   288→            )\n   289→            decision.vol_guard_state = vol_state\n   290→            decision.volatility_ok = False\n   291→            return decision\n   292→\n   293→        # Step 4: Drawdown gate multiplier\n   294→        dd_mult = self._drawdown_gate.get_multiplier()\n   295→        if dd_mult <= 0.0:\n   296→            return self._reject_trade(\n   297→                signal,\n   298→                f\"Drawdown gate halted trading (multiplier={dd_mult:.4f})\",\n   299→            )\n   300→\n   301→        # Step 5: Compute time multiplier (weekend + funding)\n   302→        time_mult = vol_state.weekend_multiplier * vol_state.funding_proximity_multiplier\n   303→\n   304→        # Step 6: Position sizing\n   305→        current_price = float(closes[current_idx])\n   306→        sizing = self._sizer.compute(\n   307→            signal_direction=signal.direction,\n   308→            confidence=signal.confidence,\n   309→            equity=self._equity,\n   310→            current_price=current_price,\n   311→            highs=highs,\n   312→            lows=lows,\n   313→            closes=closes,\n   314→            current_idx=current_idx,\n   315→            drawdown_multiplier=dd_mult,\n   316→            time_multiplier=time_mult,\n   317→            win_rate=signal.win_rate,\n   318→            payoff_ratio=signal.payoff_ratio,\n   319→        )\n   320→\n   321→        if sizing.rejected:\n   322→            return self._reject_trade(\n   323→                signal,\n   324→                sizing.rejection_reason or \"Position sizer rejected\",\n   325→            )\n   326→\n   327→        # All checks passed\n   328→        decision = TradeDecision(\n   329→            approved=True,\n   330→            quantity_btc=sizing.quantity_btc,\n   331→            notional_usd=sizing.notional_usd,\n   332→            stop_price=sizing.stop_price,\n   333→            position_fraction=sizing.position_fraction,\n   334→            reason=\"All risk checks passed\",\n   335→            sizing_details=sizing,\n   336→            kill_switch_ok=True,\n   337→            volatility_ok=True,\n   338→            drawdown_multiplier=dd_mult,\n   339→            vol_guard_state=vol_state,\n   340→        )\n   341→\n   342→        self._log_event(\n   343→            event_type=\"trade_approved\",\n   344→            direction=signal.direction,\n   345→            confidence=signal.confidence,\n   346→            approved=True,\n   347→            quantity_btc=sizing.quantity_btc,\n   348→            stop_price=sizing.stop_price,\n   349→            reason=\"all_checks_passed\",\n   350→            vol_ann=vol_state.rolling_vol_annualized,\n   351→        )\n   352→\n   353→        logger.info(\n   354→            \"trade_approved\",\n   355→            direction=signal.direction,\n   356→            confidence=round(signal.confidence, 4),\n   357→            quantity_btc=round(sizing.quantity_btc, 6),\n   358→            notional_usd=round(sizing.notional_usd, 2),\n   359→            stop_price=round(sizing.stop_price, 2),\n   360→            dd_multiplier=round(dd_mult, 4),\n   361→            vol_ann=round(vol_state.rolling_vol_annualized, 4),\n   362→        )\n   363→\n   364→        return decision\n   365→\n   366→    def on_trade_opened(\n   367→        self,\n   368→        side: str,\n   369→        quantity: float,\n   370→        entry_price: float,\n   371→        entry_time_ms: int,\n   372→        stop_price: float,\n   373→    ) -> None:\n   374→        \"\"\"Notify risk engine that a trade was executed.\n   375→\n   376→        Called by the execution layer AFTER the fill is confirmed.\n   377→        \"\"\"\n   378→        self._position.open_position(side, quantity, entry_price, entry_time_ms)\n   379→        self._last_stop_price = stop_price\n   380→        self._trades_today += 1\n   381→\n   382→    def on_trade_closed(\n   383→        self,\n   384→        exit_price: float,\n   385→        exit_time_ms: int,\n   386→    ) -> float:\n   387→        \"\"\"Notify risk engine that a position was closed. Returns realized PnL.\"\"\"\n   388→        pnl = self._position.close_position(exit_price, exit_time_ms)\n   389→\n   390→        # Update tracking\n   391→        self._daily_pnl += pnl\n   392→        self._weekly_pnl += pnl\n   393→        self._equity += pnl\n   394→\n   395→        # Update consecutive losses\n   396→        if pnl < 0:\n   397→            self._consecutive_losses += 1\n   398→        else:\n   399→            self._consecutive_losses = 0\n   400→\n   401→        # Notify drawdown gate\n   402→        self._drawdown_gate.on_trade_result(profitable=(pnl > 0))\n   403→\n   404→        # Check kill switches after the trade\n   405→        self._check_all_kill_switches()\n   406→\n   407→        logger.info(\n   408→            \"trade_closed_risk_update\",\n   409→            pnl=round(pnl, 2),\n   410→            equity=round(self._equity, 2),\n   411→            daily_pnl=round(self._daily_pnl, 2),\n   412→            consecutive_losses=self._consecutive_losses,\n   413→        )\n   414→\n   415→        return pnl\n   416→\n   417→    def on_bar(\n   418→        self,\n   419→        bar_close: float,\n   420→        bar_high: float,\n   421→        bar_low: float,\n   422→        bar_timestamp_ms: int,\n   423→        closes: NDArray[np.float64],\n   424→        highs: NDArray[np.float64],\n   425→        lows: NDArray[np.float64],\n   426→        current_idx: int,\n   427→    ) -> list[RiskAction]:\n   428→        \"\"\"Process a new bar: update state, check stops, may force exits.\n   429→\n   430→        Called on every 5-min bar by the backtest engine or live loop.\n   431→\n   432→        Returns:\n   433→            List of actions for the execution layer (empty if no action needed).\n   434→        \"\"\"\n   435→        actions: list[RiskAction] = []\n   436→\n   437→        # 1. Mark position to market\n   438→        pos = self._position.mark_to_market(bar_close, bar_timestamp_ms)\n   439→\n   440→        # 2. Update equity with unrealized PnL\n   441→        unrealized = pos.unrealized_pnl if pos.is_open else 0.0\n   442→        effective_equity = self._equity + unrealized\n   443→\n   444→        # 3. Update drawdown gate\n   445→        self._drawdown_gate.update(effective_equity)\n   446→\n   447→        # 4. Check kill switches\n   448→        self._check_all_kill_switches()\n   449→        if self._kill_switches.any_triggered() and pos.is_open:\n   450→            triggered = self._kill_switches.get_triggered_names()\n   451→            actions.append(RiskAction(\n   452→                action=RiskActionType.CLOSE_POSITION,\n   453→                reason=f\"Kill switch triggered: {', '.join(triggered)}\",\n   454→                urgency=\"immediate\",\n   455→            ))\n   456→            return actions\n   457→\n   458→        if not pos.is_open:\n   459→            return actions\n   460→\n   461→        # 5. Check max holding period\n   462→        if pos.bars_held >= self._sizer.max_holding_bars:\n   463→            actions.append(RiskAction(\n   464→                action=RiskActionType.CLOSE_POSITION,\n   465→                reason=(\n   466→                    f\"Max holding period exceeded: {pos.bars_held} bars \"\n   467→                    f\">= {self._sizer.max_holding_bars}\"\n   468→                ),\n   469→                urgency=\"high\",\n   470→            ))\n   471→            return actions\n   472→\n   473→        # 6. Check stop loss\n   474→        if self._last_stop_price > 0:\n   475→            stopped = False\n   476→            if pos.side == PositionSide.LONG and bar_low <= self._last_stop_price:\n   477→                stopped = True\n   478→            elif pos.side == PositionSide.SHORT and bar_high >= self._last_stop_price:\n   479→                stopped = True\n   480→\n   481→            if stopped:\n   482→                actions.append(RiskAction(\n   483→                    action=RiskActionType.CLOSE_POSITION,\n   484→                    reason=(\n   485→                        f\"Stop loss hit: stop={self._last_stop_price:.2f}, \"\n   486→                        f\"bar_low={bar_low:.2f}, bar_high={bar_high:.2f}\"\n   487→                    ),\n   488→                    urgency=\"immediate\",\n   489→                ))\n   490→                return actions\n   491→\n   492→        return actions\n   493→\n   494→    # -- State access ---------------------------------------------------------\n   495→\n   496→    def get_risk_state(self) -> RiskState:\n   497→        \"\"\"Return complete risk engine state for monitoring.\"\"\"\n   498→        pos = self._position.get_state()\n   499→        unrealized = pos.unrealized_pnl if pos.is_open else 0.0\n   500→\n   501→        return RiskState(\n   502→            position=pos,\n   503→            kill_switches=self._kill_switches.get_all_status(),\n   504→            drawdown_gate=self._drawdown_gate.get_state(),\n   505→            equity=self._equity + unrealized,\n   506→            daily_pnl=self._daily_pnl + unrealized,\n   507→            weekly_pnl=self._weekly_pnl + unrealized,\n   508→            consecutive_losses=self._consecutive_losses,\n   509→            trades_today=self._trades_today,\n   510→        )\n   511→\n   512→    def get_equity(self) -> float:\n   513→        \"\"\"Return current equity (realized only, no unrealized).\"\"\"\n   514→        return self._equity\n   515→\n   516→    def get_position(self) -> PositionState:\n   517→        \"\"\"Return current position state.\"\"\"\n   518→        return self._position.get_state()\n   519→\n   520→    # -- Day/week boundary management -----------------------------------------\n   521→\n   522→    def reset_daily_counters(self) -> None:\n   523→        \"\"\"Call at day boundary (00:00 UTC) to reset daily limits.\"\"\"\n   524→        logger.info(\n   525→            \"daily_counters_reset\",\n   526→            previous_daily_pnl=round(self._daily_pnl, 2),\n   527→            trades_today=self._trades_today,\n   528→        )\n   529→        self._daily_pnl = 0.0\n   530→        self._trades_today = 0\n   531→        self._position.reset_daily_pnl()\n   532→\n   533→    def reset_weekly_counters(self) -> None:\n   534→        \"\"\"Call at week boundary (Monday 00:00 UTC) to reset weekly limits.\"\"\"\n   535→        logger.info(\n   536→            \"weekly_counters_reset\",\n   537→            previous_weekly_pnl=round(self._weekly_pnl, 2),\n   538→        )\n   539→        self._weekly_pnl = 0.0\n   540→\n   541→    # Requires reason string.\"\"\"\n   545→        self._kill_switches.reset(switch_name, reason)\n   546→\n   547→    def trigger_emergency(self, reason: str) -> None:\n   548→        \"\"\"Trigger    \"emergency\": 1.0,         # always threshold=1, triggered manually\n   122→        }\n   123→\n   124→    The manager checks thresholds and triggers switches automatically.\n   125→    Reset MUST (SwitchState.TRIGGERED.value,),\n   145→        ).fetchone()\n   146→        return row[0] > 0\n   147→\n   148→    def get_triggered_names(self) -> list[SwitchName]:\n   149→        \"\"\"Return (SwitchState.TRIGGERED.value,),\n   153→        ).fetchall()\n   154→        return [row[0] for row in rows]\n   155→\n   156→    def get_all_status(self) -> list[KillSwitchStatus]:\n   157→   weekly_pnl_fraction: float,\n   201→        equity: float | None = None,\n   202→    ) -> bool:\n   203→        \"\"\"Check weekly (rolling 7-day) loss threshold.\"\"\"\n   204→        return reason=f\"Weekly loss {weekly_pnl_fraction:.4f} exceeded threshold\",\n   209→        )\n   210→\n   211→    def check_max_drawdown(\n   212→        self,\n   213→        drawdown_fraction: float,\n Single-position only (max 1 open at a time per REQUIREMENTS RR-1.2).\n   103→    - State written to SQLite on every mutation so it survives crashes.\n   104→    - Thread-safe via a reentrant lock.\n   105→    - All PnL in USD.\n   106→\n   107→    Usage (backtest):\n   108→        tracker = PositionTracker(conn)\n   109→        tracker.open_position(\"long\", 0.05, 67000.0, bar_time_ms)\n   110→        for bar in bars:\n   111→            tracker.mark_to_market(bar.close, bar.timestamp_ms)\n   112→        result = tracker.close_position(bar.close, bar.timestamp_ms)\n   113→\n   114→    Usage (live):\n   115→        tracker = PositionTracker(conn)\n   116→        # Called from order-fill callback\n   117→        tracker.open_position(\"long\", fill.qty, fill.price, fill.timestamp_ms)\n   118→        # Called every 5-min bar\n   119→        tracker.mark_to_market(bar.close, bar.timestamp_ms)\n   120→    \"\"\"\n   121→\n   122→    def __init__(self, conn: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:\n   123→        self._conn = conn\n   124→        self._lock = threading.Lock()\n   125→        self._state = PositionState()\n   126→        self._ensure_table()\n   127→        self._load_state()\n   128→\n   129→    # -- Public API -----------------------------------------------------------\n   130→\n   131→    def open_position(\n   132→        self,\n   133→        side: str,\n   134→        quantity: float,\n   135→        entry_price: float,\n   136→        entry_time_ms: int,\n   137→        symbol: str = \"BTC/USDT:USDT\",\n   138→    ) -> PositionState:\n   139→        \"\"\"Open a new position.   exit_price: Price at which to close.\n   200→            exit_time_ms: Timestamp of exit.\n   201→\n   202→        Returns:\n   203→            Realized PnL in USD for this trade.\n   204→\n   205→        Raises:\n   206→            ValueError: If no position is open.\n   207→        \"\"\"\n   208→        with self._lock:\n   209→            if not self._state.is_open:\n   210→ Uses a smooth exponential decay rather\n     5→than hard steps, so there are no cliff edges in sizing behavior.\n     6→\n     7→The multiplier curve:\n     8→    - 0% drawdown  -> 1.0x (full size)\n     9→    - 3% drawdown  -> 0.75x\n    10→    - 5% drawdown  -> 0.50x\n    11→    - 10% drawdown -> 0.25x\n    12→    - 15% drawdown -> 0.0x  (halt)\n    13→\n    14→Between these points the function interpolates smoothly using a fitted\n    15→exponential: multiplier = max(0, 1 - (dd / halt_threshold)^alpha)\n    16→where alpha is calibrated to pass through the reference points.\n    17→\n    18→Recovery logic:\n    19→    After drawdown recovers, the multiplier does NOT snap back immediately.\n    20→    A cooldown period (minimum_cooldown_bars) must elapse at the reduced\n    21→    level before the multiplier starts increasing. 129→\n   130→        Returns:\n   131→            Multiplier between 0.0 and 1.0 to scale position sizes.\n   132→        \"\"\"\n   133→        self._current_equity = equity\n   134→\n   135→ fraction\n   140→        if self._peak_equity > 0:\n   141→            dd = (self._peak_equity - equity) / self._peak_equity\n   142→        else:\n   143→            dd = 0.0\n   144→        dd = \"drawdown_gate_recovery_complete\",\n   163→                    multiplier=round(new_mult, 4),\n   164→                    drawdown=round(dd, 4),\n   165→                )\n   166→            else:\n self._recovery_wins_required\n   204→            )\n   205→        else:\n   206→            # A losing trade during recovery resets the counter\n   207→            self._recovery_wins = max(0, get_drawdown(self) -> float:\n   231→        \"\"\"Return current drawdown as positive fraction.\"\"\"\n   232→        if self._peak_equity <= 0:\n   233→            return 0.0\n   234→        return max(0.0, (self._peak_equity - self._current_equity) / self._peak_equity)\n   235→\n   236→    # -- Private helpers -------------------------------------------------------\n   237→\n   238→    def _compute_multiplier(self, drawdown: float) -> float:\n   239→        \"\"\"Compute raw multiplier from drawdown using smooth decay.\n   240→\n   241→        multiplier = max(0, 1 - (dd / halt_threshold)^alpha)\n   242→\n   243→        With alpha=1.8 and halt=0.15:\n   244→            dd=0.00 -> 1.000\n   245→            dd=0.03 -> 0.759\n   246→            dd=0.05 -> 0.592\n   247→            dd=0.10 -> 0.276\n   248→            dd=0.15 -> 0.000\n   249→        \"\"\"\n   250→        if drawdown <= 0:\n   251→            return 1.0\n   252→        if drawdown >= self._halt_threshold:\n   253→            return 0.0\n   254→\n   255→        ratio = drawdown / self._halt_threshold\n   256→        return max(0.0, 1.0 - math.pow(ratio, self._decay_alpha))\n   257→\n   258→    def _ensure_table(self) -> None:\n   259→        self._conn.execute(DRAWDOWN_GATE_TABLE)\n   260→        self._conn.commit()\n   261→\n   262→    def _persist(self) -> None:\n   263→    drawdown_scaled: float\n    52→    final_fraction: float\n    53→\n    54→    # Rejection\n    55→    rejected: bool = False\n    56→    rejection_reason: str | None = None\n    57→\n    58→\n    59→class PositionSizer:\n    60→    \"\"\"Computes position sizes using fractional Kelly criterion.\n    61→\n    62→    Configuration:\n    63→        kelly_fraction: fraction of Kelly to use (default 0.25 = quarter-Kelly)\n    64→        max_position_fraction: absolute cap on position size (default 0.05 = 5%)\n    65→        min_btc_quantity: exchange minimum order size (default 0.001)\n    66→        atr_multiplier: ATR multiple for stop loss (default 3.0)\n    67→        atr_period: bars for ATR computation (default 14)\n    68→        max_holding_bars: force exit after this many bars (default 6 = 30min)\n    69→        default_win_rate: used when no historical data (default 0.52)\n    70→        default_payoff_ratio: avg win / avg loss (default 1.0)\n    71→    \"\"\"\n    72→\n    73→    def __init__(\n    74→        self,\n    75→        kelly_fraction: float = 0.25,\n    76→        max_position_fraction: float = 0.05,\n    77→        min_btc_quantity: float = 0.001,\n    78→        atr_multiplier: float = 3.0,\n    79→        atr_period: int = 14,\n    80→        max_holding_bars: int = 6,\n    81→        default_win_rate: float = 0.52,\n    82→        default_payoff_ratio: float = 1.0,\n    83→    ) -> None:\n    84→        if not (0 < kelly_fraction <= 1):\n    85→            raise ValueError(f\"kelly_fraction must be in (0, 1], got {kelly_fraction}\")\n    86→        if not (0 < max_position_fraction <= 1):\n    87→            raise ValueError(\n    88→                f\"max_position_fraction must be in (0, 1], got {max_position_fraction}\"\n    89→            )\n    90→        if atr_multiplier <= 0:\n    91→            raise ValueError(f\"atr_multiplier must be positive, got {atr_multiplier}\")\n    92→ max_position_fraction\n    97→        self._min_btc = min_btc_quantity\n    98→        self._atr_mult = atr_multiplier\n    99→        self._atr_period = atr_period\n   100→        self._max_holding = max_holding_bars\n   101→        self._default_wr = default_win_rate\n   102→        self._default_payoff = default_payoff_ratio\n   103→\n   104→    # -- Public API -----------------------------------------------------------\n   105→\n   106→    @property\n   107→    def max_holding_bars(self) -> int:\n   108→        \"\"\"Maximum bars to hold a position before force-exit.\"\"\"\n   109→        return self._max_holding\n   110→\n   111→    def compute(\n   112→        self,\n   113→        signal_direction: str,\n   114→        confidence: float,\n   115→        equity: float,\n   116→        current_price: float,\n   117→        highs: NDArray[np.float64],\n   118→        lows: NDArray[np.float64],\n   119→        closes: NDArray[np.float64],\n   120→        current_idx: int,\n   121→        drawdown_multiplier: float = 1.0,\n   122→        time_multiplier: float = 1.0,\n   123→        win_rate: float | None = None,\n   124→        payoff_ratio: float | None = None,\n   125→    ) -> SizingResult:\n   126→        \"\"\"Compute position size for a signal.\n   127→\n   128→        Args:\n   129→            signal_direction: \"long\" or \"short\"\n   130→            confidence: Model confidence score (0.0 to 1.0)\n   131→            equity: Current total equity in USD\n   132→            current_price: Current BTC price\n   133→            highs: Array of high prices for ATR computation\n   134→            lows: Array of low prices for ATR computation\n   135→            closes: Array of close prices for ATR computation\n   136→            current_idx: Index in the price arrays\n   137→            drawdown_multiplier: From drawdown gate (0.0 to 1.0)\n   138→            time_multiplier: Weekend/funding adjustment (0.0 to 1.0)\n   139→            win_rate: Historical win rate (None = use default)\n   140→            payoff_ratio: Historical avg_win/avg_loss (None = use default)\n   141→\n   142→        Returns:\n   143→            SizingResult with quantity, stop price, and sizing breakdown.\n   144→        \"\"\"\n   145→        if signal_direction not in (\"long\", \"short\"):\n   146→            return self._rejected(f\"Invalid direction: {signal_direction}\")\n   147→        if confidence <= 0:\n   148→            return self._rejected(f\"Confidence too low: {confidence:.4f}\")\n   149→        if equity <= 0:\n   150→            return self._rejected(f\"Equity non-positive: {equity:.2f}\")\n   151→        if current_price <= 0:\n   152→            return self._rejected(f\"Price non-positive: {current_price}\")\n   153→        if drawdown_multiplier <= 0:\n   154→            return self._rejected(\"Drawdown gate halted trading (multiplier = 0)\")\n   155→\n   156→        wr = win_rate if win_rate is not None else self._default_wr\n   157→        pr = payoff_ratio if payoff_ratio is not None else self._default_payoff\n   158→\n   159→        # 1. Kelly fraction: f = (WR * payoff - (1 - WR)) / payoff\n   160→        kelly_f = self._kelly_formula(wr, pr)\n   161→        if kelly_f <= 0:\n   162→            return self._rejected(\n   163→                f\"Kelly fraction non-positive ({kelly_f:.4f}): \"\n   164→                f\"WR={wr:.3f}, payoff={pr:.3f} implies no edge\"\n   165→            )\n   166→\n   167→        # 2. Quarter-Kelly\n   168→        quarter_kelly = kelly_f * self._kelly_frac\n   169→\n   170→        # 3. Confidence scaling\n   171→        conf_scaled = quarter_kelly * confidence\n   172→\n   173→        # 4. Drawdown gate\n   174→        dd_scaled = conf_scaled * drawdown_multiplier\n   175→\n   176→        # 5. Time multiplier (weekend, funding proximity)\n   177→        time_scaled = dd_scaled * time_multiplier\n   178→\n   179→        # 6. Max cap\n   180→        final_frac = min(time_scaled, self._max_frac)\n   181→\n   182→        # 7. Convert to BTC quantity\n   183→        dollar_size = final_frac * equity\n   184→        quantity = dollar_size / current_price\n   185→\n   186→        # 8. Minimum size check\n   187→        if quantity < self._min_btc:\n   188→            return self._rejected(\n   189→                f\"Computed size {quantity:.6f} BTC below minimum {self._min_btc}\"\n   190→            )\n   191→\n   192→        # 9. ATR-based stop loss\n   193→        atr = self._compute_atr(highs, lows, closes, current_idx)\n   194→        stop_distance = self._atr_mult * atr\n   195→\n   196→        if stop_distance <= 0:\n   197→            # Fallback: use 1% of price as stop\n   198→            stop_distance = current_price * 0.01\n   199→            logger.warning(\n   200→                \"atr_fallback\",\n   201→                reason=\"ATR was zero, using 1% of price\",\n   202→                stop_distance=stop_distance,\n   203→            )\n   204→\n   205→        if signal_direction == \"long\":\n   206→            stop_price = current_price - stop_distance\n   207→        else:\n   208→            stop_price = current_price + stop_distance\n   209→\n   210→        risk_per_trade = quantity * stop_distance\n   211→\n   212→        result = SizingResult(\n   213→            quantity_btc=quantity,\n   214→            notional_usd=dollar_size,\n   215→            position_fraction=final_frac,\n   216→            stop_distance_usd=stop_distance,\n   217→            stop_price=stop_price,\n   218→            risk_per_trade_usd=risk_per_trade,\n   219→            raw_kelly_fraction=kelly_f,\n   220→            quarter_kelly_fraction=quarter_kelly,\n   221→            confidence_scaled=conf_scaled,\n   222→            drawdown_scaled=dd_scaled,\n   223→            final_fraction=final_frac,\n   224→        )\n   225→\n   226→        logger.info(\n   227→            \"position_sized\",\n   228→            direction=signal_direction,\n   229→            quantity_btc=round(quantity, 6),\n   230→            notional_usd=round(dollar_size, 2),\n   231→            fraction=round(final_frac, 4),\n   232→            stop_price=round(stop_price, 2),\n   233→            risk_usd=round(risk_per_trade, 2),\n   234→            kelly=round(kelly_f, 4),\n   235→            confidence=round(confidence, 4),\n   236→            dd_mult=round(drawdown_multiplier, 4),\n   237→        )\n   238→\n   239→        return result\n   240→\n   241→    # -- Private helpers -------------------------------------------------------\n   242→\n   243→    def _kelly_formula(self, win_rate: float, payoff_ratio: float) -> float:\n   244→        \"\"\"Kelly criterion: f = (WR * payoff - (1-WR)) / payoff.\n   245→\n   246→        Returns the optimal fraction of capital to risk.\n   247→        If negative (no edge), returns 0.\n   248→        \"\"\"\n   249→        if payoff_ratio <= 0:\n   250→            return 0.0\n   251→        f = (win_rate * payoff_ratio - (1.0 - win_rate)) / payoff_ratio\n   252→        return max(f, 0.0)\n   253→\n   254→    def _compute_atr(\n   255→        self,\n   256→        highs: NDArray[np.float64],\n   257→        lows: NDArray[np.float64],\n   258→        closes: NDArray[np.float64],\n   259→        current_idx: int,\n   260→    ) -> float:\n   261→        \"\"\"Average True Range over self._atr_period bars ending at current_idx.\n   262→\n   263→        TR = max(H-L, |H-prev_close|, |L-prev_close|)\n   264→        ATR = mean(TR) over the window.\n   265→        \"\"\"\n   266→        period = self._atr_period\n   267→        start = max(1, current_idx - period + 1)  # need previous close\n   268→        if start >= current_idx:\n   269→            return 0.0\n   270→\n   271→        tr_values: list[float] = []\n   272→        for i in range(start, current_idx + 1):\n   273→            hl = highs[i] - lows[i]\n   274→            hc = abs(highs[i] - closes[i - 1])\n   275→            lc = abs(lows[i] - closes[i - 1])\n   276→            tr_values.append(max(hl, hc, lc))\n   277→\n   278→        if not tr_values:\n   279→            return 0.0\n   280→\n   281→        return float(np.mean(tr_values))\n   282→\n   283→    def _rejected(self, reason: str) -> SizingResult:\n   284→        \"\"\"Return a zero-size result with rejection reason.\"\"\"\n   285→        logger.info(\"position_sizing_rejected\", reason=reason)\n   286→        return SizingResult(\n   287→            quantity_btc=0.0,\n   288→            notional_usd=0.0,\n   289→            position_fraction=0.0,\n   290→            stop_distance_usd=0.0,\n   291→            stop_price=0.0,\n   292→            risk_per_trade_usd=0.0,\n   293→            raw_kelly_fraction=0.0,\n   294→            quarter_kelly_fraction=0.0,\n   295→            confidence_scaled=0.0,\n   296→            drawdown_scaled=0.0,\n   297→            final_fraction=0.0,\n   298→            rejected=True,\n   299→            rejection_reason=reason,\n   300→        )\n   301→"}]},"uuid":"c80b1092-54e6-4cc7-8644-8f04b5962c1a","timestamp":"2026-03-23T13:50:45.743Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"47ad4fd6-d92f-495a-a2f7-0a38558b71ec","userType":"external","entrypoint":"claude-vscode","cwd":"/Users/edgarpocaterra/ep2-crypto","sessionId":"f48c9af0-2e30-4c92-9024-4c84a03f39db","version":"2.1.81","gitBranch":"main","slug":"spicy-gathering-plum"}

Historical Stress Scenarios\n    20→\n    21→Each scenario replays real market data through the full pipeline (features -> regime -> model -> gating -> execution). The goal is to verify the system does not blow up during known extreme events. Historical data is fetched via `scripts/collect_history.py` and stored in the backtest database.\n    22→\n    23→### 1.1 March 2020 COVID Crash (BTC -50% in 2 days)\n    24→\n    25→**What happened (March 12-13, 2020 -- \"Black Thursday\"):**\n    26→- BTC fell from ~$7,900 to ~$3,800 in roughly 36 hours (-52%).\n    27→- BitMEX alone liquidated >$1.6B in 24 hours. Aggregate cross-exchange liquidations exceeded $4B.\n    28→- Binance order book depth collapsed: top-10 bid levels lost ~80% of volume within minutes.\n    29→- Bid-ask spreads on BTCUSDT perps widened from ~0.01% to >0.5% at the worst point.\n    30→- Funding rate went deeply negative (-0.375% on Bitmex in a single 8h period) as shorts dominated.\n    31→- Volume spiked 5-10x normal -- Binance spot BTC/USDT hit 400K BTC daily volume vs ~50K normal.\n    32→- Multiple exchanges experienced API outages (BitMEX went down for ~25 minutes, which actually halted the cascade).\n    33→- The crash was correlated across all asset classes: S&P 500 -9.5% on March 12, NQ followed.\n    34→\n    35→**Setup code:**\n    36→\n    37→```python\n    38→# tests/stress/test_historical_covid_crash.py\n    39→import pytest\n    40→from datetime import datetime, timezone\n    41→from ep2_crypto.backtest.walk_forward import WalkForwardEngine\n    42→from ep2_crypto.backtest.simulator import ExecutionSimulator\n    43→from ep2_crypto.backtest.metrics import compute_all_metrics\n    44→from ep2_crypto.stress.scenario_loader import load_historical_scenario\n    45→\n    46→class TestCovidCrash:\n    47→    \"\"\"Replay March 12-13, 2020 through the full system.\"\"\"\n    48→\n    49→    @pytest.fixture\n    50→    def scenario_data(self):\n    51→        return load_historical_scenario(\n    52→            start=datetime(2020, 3, 10, tzinfo=timezone.utc),\n    53→            end=datetime(2020, 3, 15, tzinfo=timezone.utc),\n    54→            symbol=\"BTC/USDT:USDT\",\n    55→            include_orderbook=True,\n    56→            include_liquidations=True,\n    57→            include_funding=True,\n    58→            # Inject realistic conditions\n    59→            spread_multiplier=10.0,    # spreads widened ~10x\n    60→            depth_multiplier=0.2,      # book depth dropped to 20%\n    61→            slippage_multiplier=5.0,   # 5x normal slippage\n    62→        )\n    63→\n    64→    def test_max_drawdown_bounded(self, scenario_data):\n    65→        \"\"\"System must not exceed 15% drawdown (our max drawdown halt).\"\"\"\n    66→        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n    67→        assert result.max_drawdown_pct < 15.0, (\n    68→            f\"Max drawdown {result.max_drawdown_pct:.1f}% exceeded 15% limit\"\n    69→        )\n    70→\n    71→    def test_kill_switches_activate(self, scenario_data):\n    72→        \"\"\"Daily loss limit (3%) and drawdown gate must trigger.\"\"\"\n    73→        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n    74→        assert result.kill_switch_activations > 0, (\n    75→            \"Kill switches should have activated during COVID crash\"\n    76→        )\n    77→        assert result.daily_loss_limit_triggered is True\n    78→        assert result.drawdown_gate_triggered is True\n    79→\n    80→    def test_position_sizing_reduces(self, scenario_data):"}]},"uuid":"bb97ea77-a0cf-4ea1-a069-58ca70720b5c","timestamp":"2026-03-23T13:51:06.608Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"6731679c-6ffc-4dd5-8f58-fa56fa4444a4","userType":"external","entrypoint":"claude-vscode","cwd":"/Users/edgarpocaterra/ep2-crypto","sessionId":"f48c9af0-2e30-4c92-9024-4c84a03f39db","version":"2.1.81","gitBranch":"main","slug":"spicy-gathering-plum"}
