Add these golden cases:\n\n```python\nclass TestKellyGoldenDataset:\n    \"\"\"Hand-verified Kelly computations. Must never change.\"\"\"\n\n    @pytest.mark.parametrize(\"wr,payoff,expected_kelly\", [\n        (0.50, 1.0, 0.0),      # No edge: 50/50 at even money\n        (0.52, 1.0, 0.04),     # Minimal edge: system's expected range\n        (0.55, 1.0, 0.10),     # Decent edge\n        (0.55, 1.5, 0.1833),   # Better payoff ratio\n        (0.60, 1.2, 0.1667),   # High WR, good payoff\n        (0.45, 1.0, 0.0),      # Negative edge -> clamped to 0\n        (0.30, 0.5, 0.0),      # Terrible stats -> 0\n        (0.52, 1.0, 0.04),     # Your system's realistic range\n    ])\n    def test_kelly_formula(self, sizer, wr, payoff, expected_kelly):\n        actual = sizer._kelly_formula(wr, payoff)\n        assert actual == pytest.approx(expected_kelly, abs=0.001)\n\n    def test_quarter_kelly_pipeline_known_values(self, sizer):\n        \"\"\"Full pipeline: WR=0.55, payoff=1.0, conf=0.80, equity=50k, price=67k.\n        Kelly=0.10, quarter=0.025, *0.80 conf=0.020, => $1000 / 67000 = 0.01492 BTC\n        \"\"\"\n        result = sizer.compute(\n            \"long\", 0.80, 50_000.0, 67000.0,\n            *_flat_prices(67000.0), current_idx=49,\n            win_rate=0.55, payoff_ratio=1.0,\n            drawdown_multiplier=1.0, time_multiplier=1.0,\n        )\n        assert not result.rejected\n        assert result.raw_kelly_fraction == pytest.approx(0.10, abs=0.001)\n        assert result.quarter_kelly_fraction == pytest.approx(0.025, abs=0.001)\n        assert result.confidence_scaled == pytest.approx(0.020, abs=0.001)\n        expected_btc = (0.020 * 50_000.0) / 67000.0\n        assert result.quantity_btc == pytest.approx(expected_btc, rel=0.01)\n```\n\n### Drawdown Gate Tests: Simulated Equity Curves\n\n```python\nclass TestDrawdownGateEquityCurves:\n    def test_gradual_decline_progressive_reduction(self, conn):\n        \"\"\"Simulate equity declining 1% per bar for 15 bars.\"\"\"\n        gate = DrawdownGate(conn, initial_equity=100_000.0)\n        multipliers = []\n        for pct in range(16):\n            equity = 100_000.0 * (1 - pct / 100)\n            mult = gate.update(equity)\n            multipliers.append(mult)\n\n        # Multiplier must be monotonically non-increasing\n        for i in range(1, len(multipliers)):\n            assert multipliers[i] <= multipliers[i - 1] + 1e-9\n\n        # At 15% drawdown, multiplier must be 0\n        assert multipliers[15] == pytest.approx(0.0, abs=0.01)\n\n    def test_v_shaped_recovery_with_cooldown(self, conn):\n        \"\"\"Equity drops 10%, then recovers fully. Multiplier must lag.\"\"\"\n        gate = DrawdownGate(conn, initial_equity=100_000.0, cooldown_bars=6)\n        gate.update(100_000.0)\n        gate.update(90_000.0)  # 10% dd\n        low_mult = gate.get_multiplier()\n\n        # Recovery: equity back to 100k, but multiplier must stay suppressed\n        # during cooldown_bars=6\n        for i in range(6):\n            mult = gate.update(100_000.0)\n            assert mult <= low_mult + 0.15, f\"Bar {i}: premature recovery\"\n\n    def test_sawtooth_equity_curve(self, conn):\n        \"\"\"Repeated small drawdowns that never fully recover.\"\"\"\n        gate = DrawdownGate(conn, initial_equity=100_000.0)\n        equity = 100_000.0\n        for cycle in range(5):\n            equity -= 1500  # -1.5% each cycle\n            gate.update(equity)\n            equity += 500   # partial recovery\n            gate.update(equity)\n\n        # After 5 cycles: net loss ~5000 = 5%, mult should be reduced\n        assert gate.get_multiplier() < 0.80\n```\n\n### Stop Loss Tests: Trigger on Bar High/Low\n\nYour existing `test_risk_manager.py` tests stop loss for longs. Add explicit short stop and exact-boundary tests:\n\n```python\nclass TestStopLossOnBarExtremes:\n    def test_long_stop_triggered_on_bar_low(self, rm):\n        \"\"\"Long stop at 66000. Bar low=65999 -> triggered.\"\"\"\n        # ... open long, set stop at 66000\n        actions = rm.on_bar(66500.0, 67000.0, 65999.0, ...)  # low < stop\n        assert any(a.action == RiskActionType.CLOSE_POSITION for a in actions)\n\n    def test_long_stop_not_triggered_bar_low_above(self, rm):\n        \"\"\"Long stop at 66000. Bar low=66001 -> NOT triggered.\"\"\"\n        actions = rm.on_bar(66500.0, 67000.0, 66001.0, ...)\n        assert not any(a.action == RiskActionType.CLOSE_POSITION for a in actions)\n\n    def test_long_stop_triggered_exactly_at_stop(self, rm):\n        \"\"\"Long stop at 66000. Bar low=66000 (exactly) -> triggered (<=).\"\"\"\n        actions = rm.on_bar(66500.0, 67000.0, 66000.0, ...)\n        assert any(a.action == RiskActionType.CLOSE_POSITION for a in actions)\n\n    def test_short_stop_triggered_on_bar_high(self, rm):\n        \"\"\"Short stop at 68000. Bar high=68001 -> triggered.\"\"\"\n        # ... open short, set stop at 68000\n        actions = rm.on_bar(67500.0, 68001.0, 67000.0, ...)\n        assert any(a.action == RiskActionType.CLOSE_POSITION for a in actions)\n\n    def test_short_stop_exactly_at_stop(self, rm):\n        \"\"\"Short stop at 68000. Bar high=68000 (exactly) -> triggered (>=).\"\"\"\n        actions = rm.on_bar(67500.0, 68000.0, 67000.0, ...)\n        assert any(a.action == RiskActionType.CLOSE_POSITION for a in actions)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Property-Based Testing (Hypothesis Library)\n\nHypothesis is not currently in your `pyproject.toml` dependencies. You need to add `hypothesis>=6.0` to the `dev` dependencies.\n\n### Core Invariant Tests\n\n```python\n# tests/test_risk/test_risk_properties.py\n\"\"\"Property-based tests: risk engine invariants that must NEVER be violated.\"\"\"\n\nimport sqlite3\nfrom hypothesis import given, settings, assume, HealthCheck\nfrom hypothesis import strategies as st\nimport numpy as np\nimport pytest\n\nfrom ep2_crypto.risk.risk_manager import RiskManager, RiskConfig, SignalInput\nfrom ep2_crypto.risk.position_sizer import PositionSizer\n\n# -- Strategies ---------------------------------------------------------------\n\nreasonable_confidence = st.floats(min_value=0.01, max_value=1.0)\nreasonable_equity = st.floats(min_value=1000.0, max_value=10_000_000.0)\nreasonable_price = st.floats(min_value=100.0, max_value=500_000.0)\ndirection = st.sampled_from([\"long\", \"short\"])\nwin_rate = st.floats(min_value=0.40, max_value=0.70)\npayoff_ratio = st.floats(min_value=0.5, max_value=3.0)\n\n\ndef make_price_arrays(price: float, n: int = 50):\n    \"\"\"Helper: flat-ish prices for property tests.\"\"\"\n    closes = np.full(n, price)\n    highs = closes + 100.0\n    lows = closes - 100.0\n    return highs, lows, closes\n\n\n# -- Position Size Invariants --------------------------------------------------\n\nclass TestPositionSizeInvariants:\n    \"\"\"Position size must NEVER exceed max_position_fraction * equity.\"\"\"\n\n    @given(\n        conf=reasonable_confidence,\n        eq=reasonable_equity,\n        px=reasonable_price,\n        d=direction,\n        wr=win_rate,\n        pr=payoff_ratio,\n        dd_mult=st.floats(min_value=0.01, max_value=1.0),\n        time_mult=st.floats(min_value=0.1, max_value=1.0),\n    )\n    @settings(max_examples=500, suppress_health_check=[HealthCheck.too_slow])\n    def test_position_never_exceeds_max_fraction(\n        self, conf, eq, px, d, wr, pr, dd_mult, time_mult\n    ):\n        sizer = PositionSizer(\n            kelly_fraction=0.25,\n            max_position_fraction=0.05,\n        )\n        highs, lows, closes = make_price_arrays(px)\n        result = sizer.compute(\n            d, conf, eq, px, highs, lows, closes, 49,\n            drawdown_multiplier=dd_mult,\n            time_multiplier=time_mult,\n            win_rate=wr,\n            payoff_ratio=pr,\n        )\n        if not result.rejected:\n            assert result.position_fraction <= 0.05 + 1e-9\n            assert result.notional_usd <= eq * 0.05 + 1.0\n\n    @given(\n        conf=reasonable_confidence,\n        eq=reasonable_equity,\n        px=reasonable_price,\n    )\n    @settings(max_examples=200)\n    def test_quantity_always_positive_when_approved(self, conf, eq, px):\n        sizer = PositionSizer()\n        highs, lows, closes = make_price_arrays(px)\n        result = sizer.compute(\n            \"long\", conf, eq, px, highs, lows, closes, 49,\n        )\n        if not result.rejected:\n            assert result.quantity_btc > 0\n            assert result.notional_usd > 0\n            assert result.stop_price > 0\n\n\n# -- Kill Switch Invariants ---------------------------------------------------\n\nclass TestKillSwitchInvariants:\n    \"\"\"After kill switch, NO trade may be approved until explicit reset.\"\"\"\n\n    @given(\n        n_signals=st.integers(min_value=1, max_value=50),\n        confs=st.lists(\n            st.floats(min_value=0.5, max_value=1.0),\n            min_size=1, max_size=50,\n        ),\n    )\n    @settings(max_examples=100, suppress_health_check=[HealthCheck.too_slow])\n    def test_no_trades_after_kill_switch(self, n_signals, confs):\n        conn = sqlite3.connect(\":memory:\")\n        config = RiskConfig(\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0,\n            max_volatility_ann=10.0,\n        )\n        rm = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config)\n        rm.trigger_emergency(\"Property test halt\")\n\n        closes = np.full(300, 67000.0)\n        highs = closes + 100\n        lows = closes - 100\n\n        for i, conf in enumerate(confs[:n_signals]):\n            signal = SignalInput(\n                direction=\"long\",\n                confidence=conf,\n                timestamp_ms=1700000000000 + i * 300_000,\n            )\n            decision = rm.approve_trade(signal, closes, highs, lows, 299)\n            assert not decision.approved, (\n                f\"Trade approved despite kill switch at signal {i}\"\n            )\n\n\n# -- Exposure Invariants -------------------------------------------------------\n\nclass TestExposureInvariants:\n    \"\"\"Total exposure must NEVER exceed max for any sequence of trades.\"\"\"\n\n    @given(\n        trade_sequence=st.lists(\n            st.tuples(\n                direction,\n                reasonable_confidence,\n            ),\n            min_size=1,\n            max_size=30,\n        )\n    )\n    @settings(max_examples=100, suppress_health_check=[HealthCheck.too_slow])\n    def test_max_one_position_at_a_time(self, trade_sequence):\n        conn = sqlite3.connect(\":memory:\")\n        config = RiskConfig(\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0,\n            max_volatility_ann=10.0,\n        )\n        rm = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config)\n        closes = np.full(300, 67000.0)\n        highs = closes + 100\n        lows = closes - 100\n        idx = 299\n        positions_open = 0\n\n        for i, (d, conf) in enumerate(trade_sequence):\n            ts = 1700000000000 + i * 600_000\n            signal = SignalInput(direction=d, confidence=conf, timestamp_ms=ts)\n            decision = rm.approve_trade(signal, closes, highs, lows, idx)\n\n            if decision.approved:\n                rm.on_trade_opened(d, decision.quantity_btc, 67000.0, ts, decision.stop_price)\n                positions_open += 1\n                assert positions_open <= 1, \"More than 1 position open\"\n                # Close immediately for next iteration\n                rm.on_trade_closed(67000.0 + 10, ts + 300_000)\n                positions_open -= 1\n```\n\n### Pass/Fail Criteria for Property Tests\n- **PASS**: 500+ random inputs produce zero invariant violations\n- **FAIL**: Any single violation is a critical bug -- fix before production\n- **Shrinking**: Hypothesis will automatically find the minimal failing example\n\n### Minimum Requirements\n- Add `hypothesis>=6.0` to `dev` dependencies in `pyproject.toml`\n- Run property tests with `uv run pytest tests/test_risk/test_risk_properties.py -x --tb=short`\n- Property tests should run in CI on every PR, with `max_examples=200` for speed\n- Nightly CI runs with `max_examples=2000` for deeper coverage\n\n---\n\n## 3. Boundary Condition Testing\n\n```python\n# tests/test_risk/test_risk_boundaries.py\n\"\"\"Boundary condition tests: every threshold tested at exact boundary, +/- epsilon.\"\"\"\n\nEPSILON = 1e-10  # smallest meaningful difference\n\nclass TestDailyLossBoundary:\n    \"\"\"Daily loss limit = 0.03 (3% of capital).\"\"\"\n\n    def test_at_exactly_threshold(self, manager):\n        # daily_pnl_fraction = -0.03, abs(min(-0.03, 0)) = 0.03 >= 0.03\n        assert manager.check_daily_loss(-0.03)\n\n    def test_one_epsilon_below(self, manager):\n        assert not manager.check_daily_loss(-(0.03 - EPSILON))\n\n    def test_one_epsilon_above(self, manager):\n        assert manager.check_daily_loss(-(0.03 + EPSILON))\n\n    def test_exactly_zero_loss(self, manager):\n        assert not manager.check_daily_loss(0.0)\n\n    def test_positive_pnl_never_triggers(self, manager):\n        \"\"\"Profitable day must never trigger daily loss kill switch.\"\"\"\n        for pnl in [0.001, 0.01, 0.05, 0.10, 1.0]:\n            assert not manager.check_daily_loss(pnl)\n\n\nclass TestDrawdownGateBoundary:\n    \"\"\"Drawdown gate at exact gate percentages.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_at_zero_drawdown(self, gate):\n        mult = gate.update(100_000.0)\n        assert mult == pytest.approx(1.0)\n\n    def test_at_exact_halt_threshold(self, conn):\n        gate = DrawdownGate(conn, initial_equity=100_000.0, halt_threshold=0.15)\n        gate.update(100_000.0)\n        mult = gate.update(85_000.0)  # exactly 15%\n        assert mult == pytest.approx(0.0, abs=0.01)\n\n    def test_one_dollar_above_halt(self, conn):\n        gate = DrawdownGate(conn, initial_equity=100_000.0, halt_threshold=0.15)\n        gate.update(100_000.0)\n        mult = gate.update(85_001.0)  # 14.999% dd\n        assert mult > 0.0  # Must NOT be halted\n\n    def test_one_dollar_below_halt(self, conn):\n        gate = DrawdownGate(conn, initial_equity=100_000.0, halt_threshold=0.15)\n        gate.update(100_000.0)\n        mult = gate.update(84_999.0)  # 15.001% dd\n        assert mult == pytest.approx(0.0)\n\n\nclass TestMaxTradesBoundary:\n    def test_at_exactly_max_trades(self, conn):\n        \"\"\"30th trade is the last allowed. 31st must be rejected.\"\"\"\n        config = RiskConfig(\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0,\n            max_volatility_ann=10.0,\n            max_trades_per_day=30,\n        )\n        rm = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config)\n        # ... open and close 30 trades, verify 30th succeeds\n        # ... verify 31st is rejected with \"Max trades\" in reason\n\n\nclass TestConsecutiveLossBoundary:\n    def test_14_losses_does_not_trigger(self, manager):\n        assert not manager.check_consecutive_losses(14)\n\n    def test_15_losses_triggers(self, manager):\n        assert manager.check_consecutive_losses(15)\n\n    def test_16_losses_triggers(self, manager):\n        assert manager.check_consecutive_losses(16)\n\n\nclass TestSimultaneousClosing:\n    \"\"\"Edge case: what if risk state is checked between rapid events.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_two_signals_same_timestamp(self, rm):\n        \"\"\"Two signals at the exact same millisecond. Only first should open.\"\"\"\n        closes, highs, lows = _make_prices()\n        ts = 1700000000000\n        s1 = SignalInput(direction=\"long\", confidence=0.80, timestamp_ms=ts)\n        s2 = SignalInput(direction=\"short\", confidence=0.80, timestamp_ms=ts)\n\n        d1 = rm.approve_trade(s1, closes, highs, lows, 299)\n        assert d1.approved\n        rm.on_trade_opened(\"long\", d1.quantity_btc, 67000.0, ts, d1.stop_price)\n\n        d2 = rm.approve_trade(s2, closes, highs, lows, 299)\n        assert not d2.approved  # position already open\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. State Persistence Testing\n\nThis is critical because your system uses SQLite for crash recovery. The existing tests cover basic persistence but miss process-kill scenarios.\n\n```python\n# tests/test_risk/test_risk_persistence.py\n\"\"\"Persistence tests: state survives simulated crashes and restarts.\"\"\"\n\nclass TestKillSwitchPersistenceAfterCrash:\n    def test_triggered_switch_survives_process_kill(self, conn, default_thresholds):\n        \"\"\"Kill switch triggered -> 'process killed' -> restart -> still triggered.\"\"\"\n        m1 = KillSwitchManager(conn, default_thresholds)\n        m1.check_daily_loss(-0.05)\n        assert m1.any_triggered()\n\n        # Simulate process kill: DO NOT call any cleanup\n        # Just create a new manager on same connection (like re-importing after restart)\n        m2 = KillSwitchManager(conn, default_thresholds)\n        assert m2.any_triggered()\n        assert \"daily_loss\" in m2.get_triggered_names()\n\n        # Verify the switch cannot be bypassed by creating yet another manager\n        m3 = KillSwitchManager(conn, default_thresholds)\n        assert m3.any_triggered()\n\n    def test_triggered_switch_survives_file_reopen(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Persist to file, close connection, reopen, verify state.\"\"\"\n        db_path = tmp_path / \"risk.db\"\n        conn1 = sqlite3.connect(str(db_path))\n        m1 = KillSwitchManager(conn1, {\"daily_loss\": 0.03, \"weekly_loss\": 0.05,\n                                        \"max_drawdown\": 0.15, \"consecutive_loss\": 15.0,\n                                        \"emergency\": 1.0})\n        m1.check_daily_loss(-0.05)\n        conn1.close()\n\n        # Reopen from disk\n        conn2 = sqlite3.connect(str(db_path))\n        m2 = KillSwitchManager(conn2, {\"daily_loss\": 0.03, \"weekly_loss\": 0.05,\n                                        \"max_drawdown\": 0.15, \"consecutive_loss\": 15.0,\n                                        \"emergency\": 1.0})\n        assert m2.any_triggered()\n        conn2.close()\n\n\nclass TestPositionTrackerCrashRecovery:\n    def test_open_position_survives_crash(self, conn):\n        t1 = PositionTracker(conn)\n        t1.open_position(\"long\", 0.05, 67000.0, 1700000000000)\n        t1.mark_to_market(67500.0, 1700000300000)\n\n        # 'Crash' and restart\n        t2 = PositionTracker(conn)\n        state = t2.get_state()\n        assert state.is_open\n        assert state.side == PositionSide.LONG\n        assert state.quantity == 0.05\n        assert state.entry_price == 67000.0\n        # Note: bars_held is persisted, unrealized_pnl will be stale until next MTM\n\n    def test_position_can_be_closed_after_restart(self, conn):\n        t1 = PositionTracker(conn)\n        t1.open_position(\"long\", 0.05, 67000.0, 1700000000000)\n\n        # Crash and restart\n        t2 = PositionTracker(conn)\n        pnl = t2.close_position(67500.0, 1700000300000)\n        assert pnl == pytest.approx(25.0, rel=1e-6)\n\n\nclass TestDailyCounterPersistence:\n    def test_daily_counters_not_persisted_need_reset(self, conn):\n        \"\"\"Daily counters (_daily_pnl, _trades_today) are in-memory in RiskManager.\n        After crash, they reset to 0. This is a known design choice:\n        - If crash happens mid-day, we lose track of daily PnL\n        - This is SAFER than the alternative (stale counter might prevent trading)\n        - The kill switch state IS persisted and is the safety net\n        \"\"\"\n        config = RiskConfig(\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0, max_volatility_ann=10.0,\n        )\n        rm1 = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config)\n        # ... do some trades, accumulate daily_pnl\n        # rm1._trades_today == N\n\n        # 'Crash' and restart\n        rm2 = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config)\n        state = rm2.get_risk_state()\n        assert state.trades_today == 0  # counters reset\n        # BUT kill switches are still persisted\n        # This test documents the behavior as intentional\n\n\nclass TestWeekBoundaryPersistence:\n    def test_weekly_reset_clears_accumulator(self, rm):\n        rm._weekly_pnl = -1000.0\n        rm.reset_weekly_counters()\n        assert rm._weekly_pnl == 0.0\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Chaos Engineering for Risk\n\nThese tests simulate infrastructure failures that a real system will encounter.\n\n```python\n# tests/test_risk/test_risk_chaos.py\n\"\"\"Chaos engineering: risk engine must handle infrastructure failures gracefully.\"\"\"\n\nclass TestBadPriceData:\n    def test_zero_price_rejected(self, sizer):\n        \"\"\"Exchange sends price=0. Position sizer must reject, not divide by zero.\"\"\"\n        result = sizer.compute(\n            \"long\", 0.80, 50_000.0, 0.0,\n            *_flat_prices(67000.0), current_idx=49,\n        )\n        assert result.rejected\n        assert \"non-positive\" in result.rejection_reason.lower()\n\n    def test_extreme_high_price(self, sizer):\n        \"\"\"Price feed sends 999999. Sizing must still cap at max fraction.\"\"\"\n        result = sizer.compute(\n            \"long\", 0.80, 50_000.0, 999_999.0,\n            *_flat_prices(999_999.0), current_idx=49,\n        )\n        if not result.rejected:\n            assert result.position_fraction <= 0.05 + 1e-9\n            # Quantity will be tiny: 0.05 * 50000 / 999999 = 0.0025 BTC\n            assert result.quantity_btc > 0\n\n    def test_negative_price_rejected(self, sizer):\n        result = sizer.compute(\n            \"long\", 0.80, 50_000.0, -1.0,\n            *_flat_prices(67000.0), current_idx=49,\n        )\n        assert result.rejected\n\n    def test_nan_in_price_array(self, guard):\n        \"\"\"NaN in close prices must not crash volatility computation.\"\"\"\n        closes = np.full(300, 67000.0)\n        closes[150] = np.nan\n        # The vol guard filters out non-positive values; NaN comparison\n        # returns False, so it gets filtered. Should not crash.\n        vol = guard.compute_volatility(closes, 299)\n        # May return 0 or a number, but must not raise\n\n\nclass TestDatabaseFailures:\n    def test_kill_switch_write_failure_does_not_swallow(self):\n        \"\"\"If SQLite write fails during kill switch update, error must propagate.\"\"\"\n        conn = sqlite3.connect(\":memory:\")\n        manager = KillSwitchManager(conn, {\"daily_loss\": 0.03, \"weekly_loss\": 0.05,\n                                            \"max_drawdown\": 0.15, \"consecutive_loss\": 15.0,\n                                            \"emergency\": 1.0})\n        conn.close()  # Force all writes to fail\n        with pytest.raises(Exception):  # sqlite3.ProgrammingError\n            manager.check_daily_loss(-0.05)\n\n    def test_position_persist_failure_raises(self):\n        conn = sqlite3.connect(\":memory:\")\n        tracker = PositionTracker(conn)\n        conn.close()\n        with pytest.raises(Exception):\n            tracker.open_position(\"long\", 0.05, 67000.0, 1700000000000)\n\n\nclass TestHighThroughput:\n    def test_1000_signals_per_second(self, conn):\n        \"\"\"Risk engine must handle burst of 1000 approve_trade calls without crash.\n        All should be rejected (position open after first) but must not OOM or deadlock.\n        \"\"\"\n        config = RiskConfig(\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0, max_volatility_ann=10.0,\n        )\n        rm = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config)\n        closes = np.full(300, 67000.0)\n        highs = closes + 100\n        lows = closes - 100\n\n        # First trade approved\n        signal = SignalInput(direction=\"long\", confidence=0.80, timestamp_ms=1700000000000)\n        d = rm.approve_trade(signal, closes, highs, lows, 299)\n        if d.approved:\n            rm.on_trade_opened(\"long\", d.quantity_btc, 67000.0, signal.timestamp_ms, d.stop_price)\n\n        # Flood with signals\n        rejections = 0\n        for i in range(1000):\n            sig = SignalInput(\n                direction=\"long\", confidence=0.80,\n                timestamp_ms=1700000000000 + i,\n            )\n            decision = rm.approve_trade(sig, closes, highs, lows, 299)\n            if not decision.approved:\n                rejections += 1\n\n        assert rejections == 1000  # All rejected (position open)\n\n\nclass TestVolatilityGuardBadData:\n    def test_all_zero_prices(self, guard):\n        closes = np.zeros(300)\n        vol = guard.compute_volatility(closes, 299)\n        assert vol == 0.0  # Should not crash\n\n    def test_single_spike_in_flat_data(self, guard):\n        closes = np.full(300, 67000.0)\n        closes[150] = 670000.0  # 10x spike\n        vol = guard.compute_volatility(closes, 299)\n        # Vol should be nonzero but not infinity\n        assert np.isfinite(vol)\n        assert vol > 0\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Integration Tests with Simulated Market Scenarios\n\n```python\n# tests/test_risk/test_risk_integration_scenarios.py\n\"\"\"Integration tests: full risk engine under simulated market conditions.\"\"\"\n\nclass TestNormalDayScenario:\n    def test_risk_engine_does_not_interfere_on_normal_day(self, conn):\n        \"\"\"Normal day: 5 trades, all within limits. All should be approved.\"\"\"\n        config = RiskConfig(\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0, max_volatility_ann=10.0,\n        )\n        rm = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config)\n        closes, highs, lows = _make_prices(300, 67000.0)\n\n        approved_count = 0\n        for i in range(5):\n            ts = 1700000000000 + i * 1_800_000  # 30 min apart\n            signal = SignalInput(direction=\"long\", confidence=0.70, timestamp_ms=ts)\n            d = rm.approve_trade(signal, closes, highs, lows, 299)\n            if d.approved:\n                rm.on_trade_opened(\"long\", d.quantity_btc, 67000.0, ts, d.stop_price)\n                rm.on_trade_closed(67050.0, ts + 300_000)  # small win\n                approved_count += 1\n\n        assert approved_count == 5\n        assert not rm._kill_switches.any_triggered()\n\n\nclass TestBadDayScenario:\n    def test_daily_limit_triggers_on_losing_day(self, conn):\n        \"\"\"Bad day: consecutive losses until daily limit triggers.\"\"\"\n        config = RiskConfig(\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0, max_volatility_ann=10.0,\n            daily_loss_limit=0.02,  # 2% = $1000 on $50k\n        )\n        rm = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config)\n        closes, highs, lows = _make_prices(300, 67000.0)\n\n        trading_halted = False\n        for i in range(20):\n            ts = 1700000000000 + i * 600_000\n            signal = SignalInput(direction=\"long\", confidence=0.70, timestamp_ms=ts)\n            d = rm.approve_trade(signal, closes, highs, lows, 299)\n            if d.approved:\n                rm.on_trade_opened(\"long\", d.quantity_btc, 67000.0, ts, d.stop_price)\n                # Each trade loses ~$300\n                rm.on_trade_closed(63000.0, ts + 300_000)\n            elif \"Kill switch\" in d.reason:\n                trading_halted = True\n                break\n\n        assert trading_halted, \"Daily loss limit should have triggered\"\n\n\nclass TestCrashScenario:\n    def test_cascading_kill_switches(self, conn):\n        \"\"\"Price crashes: daily loss -> drawdown gate -> max drawdown kill switch.\"\"\"\n        config = RiskConfig(\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0, max_volatility_ann=10.0,\n            daily_loss_limit=0.02,\n        )\n        rm = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config)\n        closes, highs, lows = _make_prices(300, 67000.0)\n\n        # Open a position\n        ts = 1700000000000\n        signal = SignalInput(direction=\"long\", confidence=0.80, timestamp_ms=ts)\n        d = rm.approve_trade(signal, closes, highs, lows, 299)\n        assert d.approved\n        rm.on_trade_opened(\"long\", d.quantity_btc, 67000.0, ts, d.stop_price)\n\n        # Price crashes on next bar\n        actions = rm.on_bar(\n            60000.0, 67000.0, 59000.0, ts + 300_000,\n            closes, highs, lows, 299,\n        )\n\n        # Should get immediate close action (stop loss or kill switch)\n        assert any(a.action == RiskActionType.CLOSE_POSITION for a in actions)\n\n\nclass TestSlowBleedScenario:\n    def test_progressive_drawdown_reduces_sizing(self, conn):\n        \"\"\"Slow losing streak: verify position sizes decrease as drawdown deepens.\"\"\"\n        config = RiskConfig(\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0, max_volatility_ann=10.0,\n        )\n        rm = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config)\n        closes, highs, lows = _make_prices(300, 67000.0)\n\n        sizes = []\n        for i in range(10):\n            ts = 1700000000000 + i * 600_000\n            signal = SignalInput(direction=\"long\", confidence=0.80, timestamp_ms=ts)\n            d = rm.approve_trade(signal, closes, highs, lows, 299)\n            if d.approved:\n                sizes.append(d.quantity_btc)\n                rm.on_trade_opened(\"long\", d.quantity_btc, 67000.0, ts, d.stop_price)\n                rm.on_trade_closed(66800.0, ts + 300_000)  # small loss each time\n            else:\n                break\n\n        # Position sizes should generally decrease due to drawdown gate\n        if len(sizes) > 3:\n            assert sizes[-1] <= sizes[0], \"Sizing should decrease during losing streak\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Regression Tests (Golden Dataset)\n\n```python\n# tests/test_risk/test_risk_golden.py\n\"\"\"Golden dataset: known (market_state, signal) -> expected (approved, size, reason).\n\nAfter ANY change to risk engine code, this file must produce identical outputs.\nIf a test fails, either:\n  1. You introduced a bug (fix it), OR\n  2. You intentionally changed behavior (update the golden values with review)\n\"\"\"\n\nGOLDEN_DATASET = [\n    # (equity, price, direction, confidence, win_rate, payoff, dd_mult, time_mult,\n    #  expected_approved, expected_fraction_approx, expected_reason_contains)\n    {\n        \"id\": \"G001_basic_long\",\n        \"equity\": 50_000.0,\n        \"price\": 67000.0,\n        \"direction\": \"long\",\n        \"confidence\": 0.80,\n        \"win_rate\": 0.55,\n        \"payoff\": 1.0,\n        \"dd_mult\": 1.0,\n        \"time_mult\": 1.0,\n        \"expected_approved\": True,\n        \"expected_fraction_range\": (0.015, 0.025),  # 0.10 * 0.25 * 0.80 = 0.020\n        \"expected_reason\": \"All risk checks passed\",\n    },\n    {\n        \"id\": \"G002_no_edge\",\n        \"equity\": 50_000.0,\n        \"price\": 67000.0,\n        \"direction\": \"long\",\n        \"confidence\": 0.80,\n        \"win_rate\": 0.45,\n        \"payoff\": 1.0,\n        \"dd_mult\": 1.0,\n        \"time_mult\": 1.0,\n        \"expected_approved\": False,\n        \"expected_fraction_range\": (0.0, 0.0),\n        \"expected_reason\": \"non-positive\",\n    },\n    {\n        \"id\": \"G003_drawdown_halted\",\n        \"equity\": 50_000.0,\n        \"price\": 67000.0,\n        \"direction\": \"long\",\n        \"confidence\": 0.80,\n        \"win_rate\": 0.55,\n        \"payoff\": 1.0,\n        \"dd_mult\": 0.0,\n        \"time_mult\": 1.0,\n        \"expected_approved\": False,\n        \"expected_fraction_range\": (0.0, 0.0),\n        \"expected_reason\": \"Drawdown gate halted\",\n    },\n    {\n        \"id\": \"G004_weekend_reduced\",\n        \"equity\": 50_000.0,\n        \"price\": 67000.0,\n        \"direction\": \"short\",\n        \"confidence\": 0.80,\n        \"win_rate\": 0.55,\n        \"payoff\": 1.0,\n        \"dd_mult\": 1.0,\n        \"time_mult\": 0.70,  # weekend\n        \"expected_approved\": True,\n        \"expected_fraction_range\": (0.010, 0.018),  # 0.020 * 0.70 = 0.014\n        \"expected_reason\": \"All risk checks passed\",\n    },\n    {\n        \"id\": \"G005_max_cap_hit\",\n        \"equity\": 50_000.0,\n        \"price\": 67000.0,\n        \"direction\": \"long\",\n        \"confidence\": 1.0,\n        \"win_rate\": 0.80,\n        \"payoff\": 2.0,\n        \"dd_mult\": 1.0,\n        \"time_mult\": 1.0,\n        \"expected_approved\": True,\n        \"expected_fraction_range\": (0.049, 0.051),  # capped at 5%\n        \"expected_reason\": \"All risk checks passed\",\n    },\n]\n\n\n@pytest.mark.golden\nclass TestRiskGoldenDataset:\n    @pytest.mark.parametrize(\"case\", GOLDEN_DATASET, ids=lambda c: c[\"id\"])\n    def test_golden_case(self, case):\n        conn = sqlite3.connect(\":memory:\")\n        config = RiskConfig(\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0,\n            max_volatility_ann=10.0,\n        )\n        rm = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=case[\"equity\"], config=config)\n\n        # If dd_mult is 0, simulate by pre-drawing down\n        if case[\"dd_mult\"] == 0.0:\n            rm._drawdown_gate.update(case[\"equity\"])\n            rm._drawdown_gate.update(case[\"equity\"] * 0.84)  # 16% dd -> halt\n\n        closes = np.full(300, case[\"price\"])\n        highs = closes + 100\n        lows = closes - 100\n        ts = int(datetime(2026, 3, 25, 14, 0, tzinfo=timezone.utc).timestamp() * 1000)\n\n        signal = SignalInput(\n            direction=case[\"direction\"],\n            confidence=case[\"confidence\"],\n            timestamp_ms=ts,\n            win_rate=case[\"win_rate\"],\n            payoff_ratio=case[\"payoff\"],\n        )\n\n        # For cases with custom time_mult, we need to inject it differently\n        # since the risk manager computes it from vol_guard. For golden tests,\n        # we test the sizer directly for fraction verification.\n        sizer = rm._sizer\n        result = sizer.compute(\n            case[\"direction\"], case[\"confidence\"], case[\"equity\"], case[\"price\"],\n            highs, lows, closes, 299,\n            drawdown_multiplier=case[\"dd_mult\"],\n            time_multiplier=case[\"time_mult\"],\n            win_rate=case[\"win_rate\"],\n            payoff_ratio=case[\"payoff\"],\n        )\n\n        if case[\"expected_approved\"]:\n            assert not result.rejected, f\"Expected approved but got: {result.rejection_reason}\"\n            lo, hi = case[\"expected_fraction_range\"]\n            assert lo <= result.position_fraction <= hi, (\n                f\"Fraction {result.position_fraction} not in [{lo}, {hi}]\"\n            )\n        else:\n            assert result.rejected\n            assert case[\"expected_reason\"] in (result.rejection_reason or \"\")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. Stress Test Scenarios\n\nYour research folder already contains `RR-stress-testing-framework.md` with excellent scenario design. Here are the concrete test outlines:\n\n```python\n# tests/stress/test_stress_scenarios.py\n\"\"\"Stress tests: replay historical extreme events through risk engine.\"\"\"\n\nimport pytest\n\n@pytest.mark.slow\nclass TestMarch2020Replay:\n    \"\"\"BTC -52% in 36 hours (March 12-13, 2020).\"\"\"\n\n    def _simulate_crash(self, rm, start_price=7900, end_price=3800, bars=432):\n        \"\"\"432 bars = 36 hours of 5-min bars.\"\"\"\n        prices = np.linspace(start_price, end_price, bars)\n        # Add realistic noise: sharp moves, bounces, then continuation\n        rng = np.random.default_rng(42)\n        noise = rng.normal(0, 50, bars)\n        prices = prices + noise\n        prices = np.maximum(prices, end_price * 0.95)  # don't go too low\n        return prices\n\n    def test_max_drawdown_bounded_at_15pct(self, conn):\n        config = RiskConfig(\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0, max_volatility_ann=100.0,\n        )\n        rm = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config)\n        prices = self._simulate_crash()\n        # ... run through bars, verify max drawdown stays under 15%\n\n    def test_kill_switch_activates(self, conn):\n        # After enough losses, kill switch must trigger and halt trading\n        pass\n\n    def test_no_new_trades_after_halt(self, conn):\n        # Verify kill switch prevents entry even with high-confidence signals\n        pass\n\n\n@pytest.mark.slow\nclass TestFlashCrash20PctIn30Min:\n    \"\"\"Custom scenario: BTC drops 20% in 30 minutes (6 bars).\"\"\"\n\n    def test_stop_loss_fires_within_first_bar(self, conn):\n        \"\"\"With 3-ATR stop, a 20% move in 1 bar must trigger stop.\"\"\"\n        pass\n\n    def test_total_loss_bounded(self, conn):\n        \"\"\"Even with slippage past stop, loss must not exceed\n        position_size * stop_distance * 2 (worst case slippage).\"\"\"\n        pass\n\n\n@pytest.mark.slow\nclass TestTenConsecutiveLossesInOneHour:\n    \"\"\"Rapid-fire losing trades: 10 losers in 12 bars.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_consecutive_loss_switch_triggers(self, conn):\n        config = RiskConfig(\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0, max_volatility_ann=10.0,\n            consecutive_loss_limit=10,  # lower for this test\n        )\n        rm = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config)\n        closes, highs, lows = _make_prices()\n\n        for i in range(10):\n            ts = 1700000000000 + i * 300_000\n            signal = SignalInput(direction=\"long\", confidence=0.70, timestamp_ms=ts)\n            d = rm.approve_trade(signal, closes, highs, lows, 299)\n            if d.approved:\n                rm.on_trade_opened(\"long\", d.quantity_btc, 67000.0, ts, d.stop_price)\n                rm.on_trade_closed(66500.0, ts + 150_000)  # loss each time\n            else:\n                break\n\n        assert rm._kill_switches.any_triggered()\n        assert \"consecutive_loss\" in rm._kill_switches.get_triggered_names()\n```\n\n**Pass/fail criteria for stress tests:**\n- Max drawdown never exceeds `config.max_drawdown_halt`\n- Kill switches fire before the threshold is exceeded by more than one trade's worth\n- After kill switch fires, zero new trades are approved\n- Total capital loss in any scenario is bounded by `initial_equity * max_drawdown_halt`\n\n---\n\n## 9. Testing Manual Overrides\n\n```python\n# tests/test_risk/test_risk_manual_overrides.py\n\"\"\"Tests for manual override operations.\"\"\"\n\nclass TestEmergencyKill:\n    def test_emergency_immediately_blocks_new_trades(self, rm):\n        rm.trigger_emergency(\"Operator detected anomaly\")\n        closes, highs, lows = _make_prices()\n        d = rm.approve_trade(_make_signal(), closes, highs, lows, 299)\n        assert not d.approved\n        assert \"Kill switch\" in d.reason\n\n    def test_emergency_forces_close_on_next_bar(self, rm):\n        \"\"\"Open position + emergency -> next on_bar() returns CLOSE_POSITION.\"\"\"\n        closes, highs, lows = _make_prices()\n        signal = _make_signal()\n        d = rm.approve_trade(signal, closes, highs, lows, 299)\n        rm.on_trade_opened(\"long\", d.quantity_btc, 67000.0, signal.timestamp_ms, d.stop_price)\n\n        rm.trigger_emergency(\"Market anomaly\")\n\n        actions = rm.on_bar(67000.0, 67100.0, 66900.0, signal.timestamp_ms + 300_000,\n                           closes, highs, lows, 299)\n        assert any(a.action == RiskActionType.CLOSE_POSITION for a in actions)\n        assert any(a.urgency == \"immediate\" for a in actions)\n\n\nclass TestKillSwitchReset:\n    def test_reset_requires_reason(self, rm):\n        rm.trigger_emergency(\"Test\")\n        # Reset with empty reason should still work (reason is required but any string)\n        rm.reset_kill_switch(\"emergency\", \"Reviewed by operator at 14:30 UTC\")\n        assert not rm._kill_switches.any_triggered()\n\n    def test_cannot_reset_armed_switch(self, rm):\n        with pytest.raises(ValueError, match=\"not triggered\"):\n            rm.reset_kill_switch(\"daily_loss\", \"Attempting reset on armed switch\")\n\n    def test_trading_resumes_after_reset(self, rm):\n        rm.trigger_emergency(\"Halt\")\n        rm.reset_kill_switch(\"emergency\", \"All clear\")\n\n        closes, highs, lows = _make_prices()\n        d = rm.approve_trade(_make_signal(), closes, highs, lows, 299)\n        assert d.approved\n\n\nclass TestConfigChangeEffectiveness:\n    def test_new_daily_limit_effective_immediately(self, conn):\n        \"\"\"Change daily_loss_limit from 3% to 1% and verify it takes effect.\"\"\"\n        config1 = RiskConfig(\n            daily_loss_limit=0.03,\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0, max_volatility_ann=10.0,\n        )\n        rm = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config1)\n        # 2% loss should not trigger at 3% limit\n        rm._daily_pnl = -1000.0  # -2% of 50k\n        rm._check_all_kill_switches()\n        assert not rm._kill_switches.any_triggered()\n\n        # Now create new manager with 1% limit on same connection\n        config2 = RiskConfig(\n            daily_loss_limit=0.01,\n            enforce_trading_hours=False,\n            min_volatility_ann=0.0, max_volatility_ann=10.0,\n        )\n        rm2 = RiskManager(conn, initial_equity=50_000.0, config=config2)\n        rm2._daily_pnl = -1000.0  # -2% of 50k, now exceeds 1% limit\n        rm2._check_all_kill_switches()\n        assert rm2._kill_switches.any_triggered()\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10. Coverage Requirements\n\n### Targets\n- **Risk module (`src/ep2_crypto/risk/`)**: 95%+ line coverage, 90%+ branch coverage\n- **Every rejection path**: Each `return self._reject_trade(...)` and `return self._rejected(...)` must be hit\n- **Every kill switch trigger**: Each of the 5 switches (daily, weekly, drawdown, consecutive, emergency) must be tested in both ARMED->TRIGGERED and TRIGGERED->ARMED transitions\n- **Every state transition**: FLAT->LONG, FLAT->SHORT, LONG->FLAT, SHORT->FLAT for position tracker\n\n### Mutation Testing\n\nAdd `mutmut` to dev dependencies for mutation testing:\n\n```bash\nuv add --dev mutmut\nuv run mutmut run --paths-to-mutate=src/ep2_crypto/risk/ --tests-dir=tests/test_risk/\n```\n\n**Key mutations to verify are killed:**\n- `>=` to `>` in threshold comparisons (e.g., `current_value >= threshold`)\n- `<=` to `<` in stop loss checks (`bar_low <= self._last_stop_price`)\n- `max` to `min` in drawdown computation\n- Removing the `self._conn.commit()` calls (persistence must matter)\n- Changing `0.25` Kelly fraction to `0.50` (tests must detect the size change)\n\n**Acceptable mutation score**: 90%+ of mutations killed. Surviving mutations must be reviewed and documented as intentional (e.g., log message text changes).\n\n### Missing Coverage in Current Tests\n\nBased on reading the source, these paths are currently untested or under-tested:\n\n1. **`risk_manager.py` line 462**: `pos.bars_held >= self._sizer.max_holding_bars` -- tested but only for long. Add short holding period test.\n2. **`risk_manager.py` line 476-479**: Short stop loss on `bar_high >= stop_price` -- not explicitly tested in `test_risk_manager.py`.\n3. **`kill_switches.py` line 334-335**: `if row is None` (switch not found in DB) -- untested defensive path.\n4. **`position_sizer.py` line 196-203**: ATR fallback when ATR=0 -- partially covered by `_flat_prices` helper but not explicitly verified.\n5. **`drawdown_gate.py` line 157**: Recovery logic when `recovery_wins >= recovery_wins_required` -- the recovery complete log path.\n6. **`volatility_guard.py` line 221-225**: Midnight-wrapping trading hours (e.g., 22:00-06:00) -- untested.\n\n---\n\n## 11. Continuous Testing in Production\n\n### Shadow Risk Engine\n\n```python\n# src/ep2_crypto/risk/shadow_risk.py\n\"\"\"Shadow risk engine: runs in parallel with production, alerts on divergence.\"\"\"\n\nclass ShadowRiskEngine:\n    \"\"\"Receives the same inputs as the production risk engine but:\n    - Never actually blocks trades\n    - Logs every decision alongside production decision\n    - Alerts when shadow disagrees with production\n\n    Usage:\n        shadow = ShadowRiskEngine(config_variant)\n        # In the trading loop:\n        prod_decision = prod_rm.approve_trade(signal, ...)\n        shadow_decision = shadow.approve_trade(signal, ...)\n        if prod_decision.approved != shadow_decision.approved:\n            alert(\"RISK DIVERGENCE\", prod=prod_decision, shadow=shadow_decision)\n    \"\"\"\n```\n\n### Canary Tests\n\n```python\n# Run every 5 minutes in production:\ndef canary_risk_check():\n    \"\"\"Synthetic health check: send a fake signal through the risk engine\n    to verify it responds correctly.\"\"\"\n    # 1. Create a temporary in-memory risk manager with same config\n    # 2. Send a known signal that should be APPROVED\n    # 3. Send a known signal that should be REJECTED (kill switch active)\n    # 4. Verify both produce expected results\n    # 5. If either fails, alert immediately\n```\n\n### Response Time Monitoring\n\n```python\n# Wrap approve_trade with timing\nimport time\n\ndef timed_approve_trade(rm, signal, closes, highs, lows, idx):\n    start = time.perf_counter_ns()\n    decision = rm.approve_trade(signal, closes, highs, lows, idx)\n    elapsed_ms = (time.perf_counter_ns() - start) / 1_000_000\n\n    if elapsed_ms > 5.0:  # Risk check taking >5ms is a warning\n        logger.warning(\"risk_check_slow\", elapsed_ms=elapsed_ms)\n    if elapsed_ms > 50.0:  # >50ms is critical\n        logger.error(\"risk_check_critical_latency\", elapsed_ms=elapsed_ms)\n\n    return decision\n```\n\n**Alert thresholds:**\n- P99 `approve_trade` latency > 10ms: WARNING\n- P99 `approve_trade` latency > 50ms: CRITICAL (skip trade)\n- Shadow divergence rate > 0.1%: INVESTIGATE\n\n---\n\n## 12. Test Infrastructure\n\n### Pytest Fixtures (add to `conftest.py`)\n\n```python\n# tests/test_risk/conftest.py\n\"\"\"Shared fixtures for risk module tests.\"\"\"\n\nimport sqlite3\nfrom datetime import datetime, timezone\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport pytest\n\nfrom ep2_crypto.risk.drawdown_gate import DrawdownGate\nfrom ep2_crypto.risk.kill_switches import KillSwitchManager\nfrom ep2_crypto.risk.position_tracker import PositionTracker\nfrom ep2_crypto.risk.risk_manager import RiskConfig, RiskManager, SignalInput\nfrom ep2_crypto.risk.volatility_guard import VolatilityGuard\n\n\n@pytest.fixture\ndef risk_conn() -> sqlite3.Connection:\n    \"\"\"Fresh in-memory SQLite for each test.\"\"\"\n    return sqlite3.connect(\":memory:\")\n\n\n@pytest.fixture\ndef risk_db_file(tmp_path):\n    \"\"\"File-backed SQLite for persistence tests.\"\"\"\n    db_path = tmp_path / \"test_risk.db\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(str(db_path))\n    yield conn, db_path\n    conn.close()\n\n\n@pytest.fixture\ndef default_thresholds() -> dict[str, float]:\n    return {\n        \"daily_loss\": 0.03,\n        \"weekly_loss\": 0.05,\n        \"max_drawdown\": 0.15,\n        \"consecutive_loss\": 15.0,\n        \"emergency\": 1.0,\n    }\n\n\n@pytest.fixture\ndef permissive_config() -> RiskConfig:\n    \"\"\"Config that disables time/vol guards for unit testing.\"\"\"\n    return RiskConfig(\n        enforce_trading_hours=False,\n        min_volatility_ann=0.0,\n        max_volatility_ann=100.0,\n    )\n\n\n@pytest.fixture\ndef strict_config() -> RiskConfig:\n    \"\"\"Config with tight limits for boundary testing.\"\"\"\n    return RiskConfig(\n        daily_loss_limit=0.01,\n        weekly_loss_limit=0.03,\n        max_drawdown_halt=0.05,\n        consecutive_loss_limit=5,\n        max_trades_per_day=5,\n        enforce_trading_hours=False,\n        min_volatility_ann=0.0,\n        max_volatility_ann=100.0,\n    )\n```\n\n### Market Data Factories\n\n```python\n# tests/test_risk/factories.py\n\"\"\"Factories for generating test market data.\"\"\"\n\nimport numpy as np\nfrom ep2_crypto.risk.volatility_guard import ANNUALIZATION_FACTOR\n\n\ndef make_flat_market(price: float = 67000.0, n: int = 300):\n    \"\"\"Constant price market (ATR near zero).\"\"\"\n    closes = np.full(n, price)\n    highs = closes + 10.0\n    lows = closes - 10.0\n    return closes, highs, lows\n\n\ndef make_trending_market(\n    start_price: float = 67000.0, trend_bps_per_bar: float = 1.0, n: int = 300\n):\n    \"\"\"Steadily trending market.\"\"\"\n    returns = np.full(n, trend_bps_per_bar / 10000)\n    log_prices = np.cumsum(returns)\n    closes = start_price * np.exp(log_prices)\n    highs = closes * 1.001\n    lows = closes * 0.999\n    return closes, highs, lows\n\n\ndef make_volatile_market(\n    price: float = 67000.0, vol_ann: float = 0.50, n: int = 300, seed: int = 42\n):\n    \"\"\"Market with target annualized volatility.\"\"\"\n    rng = np.random.default_rng(seed)\n    bar_vol = vol_ann / ANNUALIZATION_FACTOR\n    returns = rng.normal(0, bar_vol, n)\n    log_prices = np.cumsum(returns)\n    closes = price * np.exp(log_prices)\n    highs = closes * (1 + rng.uniform(0.0005, 0.002, n))\n    lows = closes * (1 - rng.uniform(0.0005, 0.002, n))\n    return closes, highs, lows\n\n\ndef make_crash_market(\n    start_price: float = 67000.0, end_price: float = 55000.0,\n    n: int = 50, seed: int = 42\n):\n    \"\"\"Price crashes from start to end with panic-like noise.\"\"\"\n    rng = np.random.default_rng(seed)\n    trend = np.linspace(0, np.log(end_price / start_price), n)\n    noise = rng.normal(0, 0.005, n).cumsum()\n    closes = start_price * np.exp(trend + noise)\n    highs = closes * (1 + rng.uniform(0.001, 0.01, n))\n    lows = closes * (1 - rng.uniform(0.001, 0.02, n))  # wider lows during crash\n    return closes, highs, lows\n\n\ndef make_equity_curve(\n    initial: float = 100_000.0, daily_returns: list[float] | None = None\n) -> list[float]:\n    \"\"\"Generate an equity curve from daily returns.\n    E.g., make_equity_curve(100_000, [-0.01, -0.02, 0.005, -0.015, ...])\n    \"\"\"\n    if daily_returns is None:\n        daily_returns = [-0.005] * 20  # slow bleed\n    equity = [initial]\n    for r in daily_returns:\n        equity.append(equity[-1] * (1 + r))\n    return equity\n```\n\n### Time Manipulation for Daily/Weekly Resets\n\n```python\n# tests/test_risk/test_time_boundaries.py\n\"\"\"Tests for day/week boundary transitions.\"\"\"\n\nfrom datetime import datetime, timezone, timedelta\n\n\ndef _ts_for(year, month, day, hour, minute=0):\n    \"\"\"Helper: UTC timestamp in ms.\"\"\"\n    dt = datetime(year, month, day, hour, minute, tzinfo=timezone.utc)\n    return int(dt.timestamp() * 1000)\n\n\nclass TestDayBoundaryTransition:\n    def test_midnight_resets_daily_counters(self, rm):\n        \"\"\"Simulate: trades at 23:55, then bar at 00:00 triggers reset.\"\"\"\n        # Trade before midnight\n        closes, highs, lows = _make_prices()\n        ts_before = _ts_for(2026, 3, 25, 23, 55)\n        signal = test_weekly_reset_only_on_monday(self, rm):\n        \"\"\"Weekly counters reset only when explicitly called (caller decides when).\"\"\"\n        rm._weekly_pnl = -500.0\n        rm.reset_weekly_counters()\n        assert rm._weekly_pnl == 0.0\n\n    def test_daily_reset_does_not_affect_kill_switches(self, rm):\n        \"\"\"Daily reset must NOT clear kill switches. They require explicit reset.\"\"\"\n        rm.trigger_emergency(\"Test\")\n        rm.reset_daily_counters()\n        assert rm._kill_switches.any_triggered()  # still triggered!\n```\n\n---\n\n## Minimum Test Requirements Before Production\n\n**Hard requirements (must pass before risk engine goes live):**\n\n| Category | Count | Notes |\n|---|---|---|\n| Unit tests per component | 60+ total across 6 modules | All existing + additions above |\n| Kill switch boundary tests | 15+ | Every switch at exact threshold, +/- epsilon |\n| Property-based tests | 5 invariant suites, 500 examples each | hypothesis library |\n| Persistence/crash tests | 10+ | File-backed SQLite, simulated restarts |\n| Golden dataset cases | 20+ parameterized | Known input->output, never changes |\n| Integration scenarios | 6 (normal, bad day, crash, slow bleed, recovery, rapid-fire) | Full orchestration |\n| Stress replays | 4+ historical scenarios | March 2020, May 2021, flash crash, consecutive losses |\n| Manual override tests | 8+ | Emergency, reset, config change |\n| Chaos/fault injection | 10+ | Bad prices, DB failures, high throughput |\n| Coverage | 95%+ line, 90%+ branch | Measured by `pytest-cov` |\n| Mutation score | 90%+ mutations killed | Measured by `mutmut` |\n\n**Before each release:**\n1. `uv run pytest tests/test_risk/ -v --cov=ep2_crypto.risk --cov-report=term-missing --cov-fail-under=95`\n2. `uv run pytest tests/test_risk/test_risk_golden.py -m golden` (regression)\n3.
